tāni śīghram prayaccha me samāyāhi vicārya ettham śaraṇam devataiḥ saha iti dūta vacaḥ śrutvā vismitaḥ tridaśādhipaḥ adrayaḥ mad bhayāt ca etāḥ sva kukṣi sthāḥ yatas kṛtāḥ anye api mad bhṛtyaiḥ te rakṣitāḥ ditijāḥ purā tasmāt ratna jātam tu mayā sarvam hṛtam kila śaṃkhaḥ api evam purā daityaḥ mām dṛṣṭvā sāgara ātmajaḥ mama anujena hariṇā nihataḥ sa hi pāpa dhīḥ hiṃsakaḥ sādhu saṃghasya pāpiṣṭhaḥ sāgaraḥ tat gaccha dūta śīghram tvam kathayasva asya tattvataḥ tadā indreṇa agamat tūrṇam yatra vīraḥ jalaṃdharaḥ udyogam akarot tūrṇam sarva deva jigīṣayā ditijāḥ pratyapadyanta koṭiśas koṭiśas tathā atha śuṃbha niśuṃbha ādyaiḥ bala adhipati koṭibhiḥ nirjagāma mahā vīraḥ sindhu putraḥ pratāpavān prāpa triviṣṭapam sadyas sarva sainya samāvṛtaḥ dadhmau śaṃkham jalaṃdhijaḥ neduḥ vīrāḥ ca sarvatas gatvā triviṣṭapam daityaḥ nandana adhi sthitaḥ abhavat sarva sainyam samāvṛtya kurvāṇaḥ siṃha vat ravam puram āvṛtya tiṣṭhat tat ṛṣṭvā sainya balam mahat niryayuḥ tu amarāvatyāḥ devāḥ yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ musalaiḥ parighaiḥ bāṇaiḥ gadā paraśu śaktibhiḥ patitaiḥ pātyamānaiḥ ca gaja aśva ratha pattibhiḥ devān api tathā yuddhe tatra ājīvaya girāḥ divyauṣadhaiḥ samānīya droṇā dreḥ sa punar punar dṛṣṭavān sa tathā yuddhe punar eva samutthitān jalaṃdharaḥ krodha vaśaḥ bhārgavam vākyam abravīt mayā devāḥ hatāḥ yuddhe uttiṣṭhati katham punar tatas saṃjīvinī vidyā na eva anyatra iti vai śrutā śukraḥ uvāca divya oṣadhīḥ samāṃnīya droṇa adreḥ aṃgirāḥ surān jīvayati eṣa vai tāta satyam jānīhi me vacaḥ jayam icchasi ced tāta śṛṇu me vacanam śubham tatas saḥ aram bhujābhyām tvam droṇam abdhau upāhara drutam jagāma yatra asau āste ca eva adrirāj ca saḥ bhujābhyām tarasā daityaḥ nītvā droṇam ca tam tadā prākṣipat sāgare tūrṇam citram na hara tejasi jaghāna astraiḥ ca vividhaiḥ surān kṛtvā balam mahat atha devān hatān dṛṣṭvā droṇāt vimagamat varuḥ tāvat tatra giri iṃdra tam na dadarśa sura ācitaḥ jñātvā daitya hṛtam droṇa ghiṣaṇaḥ bhaya vihvalaḥ āgatya devān provāca jīvaḥ vyākula mānasaḥ palāyadhvam surāḥ sarve droṇaḥ na asti giriḥ mad dānam jalaṃdharaḥ mahā daityaḥ na ayam jetum kṣamaḥ yatas rudra aṃśa saṃbhavaḥ hi eṣa sarva amara vimardanaḥ mayā jñātaḥ śi śiva apamāna smarata akhilam śrutvā tad vacanam devāḥ surā ca ārya prakīrtitam jaya āśām tyaktavaṃtaḥ te bhaya vihvalitāḥ tathā detya rājena tena atihanyamānāḥ samaṃtataḥ dhairya tyaktvā apalāyanta diśaḥ daśa sa vāsavāḥ devān vidrāvitān dṛṣṭvā daityāḥ sāgara naṃdanaḥ śaṃkha bherī ja yavaiḥ praviveśa amarāvatīm praviṣṭe nagarīm daitye devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ suvarṇāt viguhām prāptāḥ nyavasan daitya tāpitāḥ śuṃbha ādikān daitya varān pṛthak pṛthak svayam suvarṇa ādi guhām vyagāt sune iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdharavadhopākhyāne devajalaṃdharayuddhavarṇanam nāma paṃcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ punar daityam samāyātam dṛṣṭvā devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ te surāḥ natvā sa prajāpatayaḥ ukhilāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ hṛṣīkeśa mahā bāho bhagavat madhusūdana matsya rūpāya te viṣṇo vedān nītavateḥ namaḥ satyavatena sat rājñā pralaya abdhi vihāriṇe kurvāṇānām surāṇām ca maṃthanāya udyamam bhṛśam bibhrate maṃdara girim kūrma rūpāya te namaḥ vasuṃdharā jana ādhārām mūrddhataḥ bibhrate namaḥ namaḥ paraśurāmāya kṣatra niḥkṣatra kāriṇe mātuḥ hita kṛte tubhyam kupitāya asatām he rāmāya loka rāmāya maryādāpuruṣāya te rāvaṇa anta karāya āśu sītāyāḥ pataye namaḥ namaḥ te jñāna gūḍhāya kṛṣṇāya paramātmane rādhā vihāra śīlāya nānā līlā karāya ca namaḥ te gūḍha dehāya veda niṃdā karāya ca yoga ācāryāya jaināya bauddha rūpāya māpate namaḥ te kalki rūpāya mlecchānām aṃta kāriṇe vadate sāṃkhya yogam ca sāṃkhya ācāryāya vai prabho namaḥ paramahaṃsāya jñānam saṃvadate param vidhātre jñāna rūpāya yena ātmā saṃprasīdati vedavyāsāya vedānām vibhāgam kurvate namaḥ hitāya sarva sarva lokānām purāṇa racanāya ca āhitre sva dāsānām sukha dāya śubhāya ca pītāmbarāya haraye tārkṣya yānāya te namaḥ śeṣa talpa śaya ayāka kṛpā sindho ramānātha pāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān jalaṃdhareṇa devāḥ ca svargāt sarve nirākṛtāḥ pātālāt nāga rājaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ nirākṛtaḥ vicaranti yathā martyāḥ śobhaṃte na eva te surāḥ śaraṇam te vayam prāptāḥ vadhaḥ tasya vicityatām iti dīna vacaḥ śrutvā devānām madhusūdanaḥ jagāda karuṇā sindhuḥ megha nirhrādayā girā viṣṇuḥ uvāca ārohat garuḍam vegāt kṛpayā bhakta vatsalaḥ gacchantam vallabham dṛṣṭvā devaiḥ sārddham samudrajā sa aṃjaliḥ bāṣpa nayanā lakṣmī vacanam abravīt lakṣmī uvāca viṣṇuḥ uvāca rudra aṃśa saṃbhava tvāt ca brahmaṇaḥ vacanāt api iti uktvā garuḍa ārūḍhaḥ śaṃkha cakra gadā asi bhṛt viṣṇuḥ vegāḥ dyayau yoddhum devaiḥ śakra ādibhiḥ saha atha aruṇāḥ nuja java pakṣa vāta prapīḍitāḥ vātyā vivartitāḥ daityāḥ babhramuḥ khe yathā ghanāḥ tatas jalaṃdharaḥ dṛṣṭvā daityān vātyā prapīḍitān uddhṛtya vacanam krodhāt drutam viṣṇum samabhyagāt tejasā ca hareḥ puṣṭāḥ mahā bala samanvitāḥ daityān ājñāpayāmāsa samare ca ati durmadān mauryāḥ stu lakṣa saṃkhyātāḥ dhaumrāḥ hi śata saṃkhyakāḥ asurāḥ koṭi saṃkhyātāḥ kālakeyāḥ tathā eva ca kālakānām dauhṛdānām kaṃkānām lakṣa saṃkhyayā sarve sajjāḥ viniryāta bahu senā abhi saṃyutāḥ nānā śastra astra saṃyuktāḥ nirbhayāḥ gata saṃśayāḥ bho bhoṃ śuṃbha niśuṃbhau ca devān samara kātarān kṣaṇena su mahā vīryau tucchān nāśayatam yuvām daityāḥ jalaṃdhara ājñaptāḥ ittham yuddha viśāradāḥ gadābhiḥ tīkṣṇa bāṇaiḥ ca śūla paṭṭiśa tomaraiḥ devāḥ tathā mahā vīrāḥ hṛṣīkeśa bala anvitāḥ yuyudhuḥ tīkṣṇa bāṇāḥ ca kṣipaṃtaḥ siha vat ravāḥ kecid vāṇaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ ca kecid musala tomaraiḥ ittham surāṇām daityānām saṃgrāmaḥ samabhūt mahān atyulbaṇaḥ om munīnām hi siddhānām bhaya kārakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīya rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe devayuddhavarṇanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha daityāḥ mahā vīryāḥ śūlaiḥ paraśu paṭṭiśaiḥ daitya āyudhaiḥ samāviddha dehāḥ devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ raṇāt vidudruvuḥ sarve bhaya vyākula mānasāḥ palāyana parān dṛṣṭvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ surān atha viṣṇuḥ vai garuḍa ārūḍhaḥ yoddhum abhyāyayau drutam reje bhakta abhayaṃkaraḥ śaṃkha khaṅga gadā śārṅga dhārī krodha samanvitaḥ kaṭhorātraḥ mahā vīraḥ sarva yuddha viśāradaḥ visphūryam vinanāda ha śārṅga nismṛta bāṇaiḥ ca ditijānām śirāṃsi vai cakartta bhagavān viṣṇuḥ koṭiśas ruṭ samākulaḥ atha aruṇa anuja java pakṣa vāta prapīḍitāḥ vātyā vivarttitāḥ daityāḥ babhramuḥ khe yathā ghanāḥ tatas jalaṃdharaḥ dṛṣṭvā daityān vātyā prapīḍitān caḥ tam dṛṣṭvā daityān prasphurita adharaḥ sa cakāra mahā nādam deva asura bhayaṃkaram daityānām adhipaḥ vidīrṇāḥ śravaṇāt tatas bhayaṅkareṇa daityasya nādena pūritam tadā ākāśam kurvatoḥ bāṇaiḥ tadā niravakāśa vat deva asura ṛṣi siddhānām bhīkareṇa ati vismayaḥ viṣṇuḥ daityasya bāṇa oghaiḥ dhvajam chatram dhanuḥ śarān ciccheda tam ca hṛdaye bāṇena ekena tāḍayan āhatya garuḍam mūrdhni pātayāmāsa bhū tale viṣṇum jaghāna śūlena tīkṣṇena prasphuraḍhucā tam vivyādha śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śārṅgam visphūrya daitya hā viṣṇuḥ jalaṃdharam daityam bhaya dena śareṇa ha krodha āviṣṭaḥ ati tīkṣṇena jaghāna āśu surāri hā āgatam tasya tam bāṇam dṛṣṭvā daityaḥ mahā balaḥ chittvā bāṇena viṣṇum ca jaghāna hṛdaye drutam keśavaḥ api mahā bāhum vikṣiptam asureṇa tam śaram tila pramāḥ ṇena chittvā vīraḥ nanāda ha punar bāṇam samādhatta dhanuṣi krodha vepitaḥ vāsudevaḥ punar bāṇam nāśāya vibudha dviṣaḥ śareṇa svena śākhyam puṃstvam aṣim punar bāṇaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ca jaghāna madhusūdanam ugra vīryaḥ mahā vīraḥ devānām bhaya kārakaḥ jalaṃdharasya nāśāya cikṣepa sva gadām parām sā gadā hariṇā kṣiptā jvalat jvalana sannibhā jalaṃdharaḥ mada unmattaḥ puṣpa mālā hataḥ yathā triśūlam anala ākāram haraye raṇa durmmadaḥ nandaka ākhyena khaṅgena smṛtvā śiva pada ambujam āgatya hṛdaye viṣṇum jaghāna dṛḍha muṣṭinā saḥ api viṣṇuḥ ma hāvīraḥ a vigaṇayya ca tad vyathām jalaṃdharam ca hṛdaye jaghāna dṛḍha muṣṭinā bāhubhiḥ muṣṭibhiḥ ca eva jānu bhiḥ nādayan mahīm evam hi su ciram yuddham kṛtvā tena asureṇa vai vismitaḥ abhūt muni śreṣṭha hṛdi glānim avāpa ha atha prasannaḥ bhagavān māyī māyā vidām varaḥ uvāca daitya rājānam megha gaṃbhīrayā girā viṣṇuḥ uvāca mahā ājau durmadāḥ vīrāḥ chinna dehāḥ mṛtim gatāḥ iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya viṣṇoḥ māyāvinaḥ hareḥ uvāsa sva ālayam prāptaḥ harṣa ākulita mānasaḥ jalam dharaḥ atha devānām adhikāreṣu dānavān sthāpayitvā sa harṣaḥ san punar āgāt mahī talam tat ātma vaśagam kṛtvā atiṣṭhat sāgaranaṃdanaḥ pātāla bhavane daityam niśuṃbham su mahā balam sthāpayitvā sa śeṣa ādīn ānayat bhū talam balī sarpa rākṣasa mānuṣān sva pure nāgarān kṛtvā śaśāsa bhuvanatrayam evam jalaṃdharaḥ kṛtvā devān sva vaśa vartinaḥ dharmeṇa pālayāmāsa prajāḥ pṛthakkartṛ tvam āśritya ekavacanam na dīnaḥ dṛśyate tasmin dharmāt rājyam praśāsati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdhara upākhyāne viṣṇujalaṃdharayuddhavarṇanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ evam śāsati dharmeṇa mahīm tasmin mahā asure babhūvuḥ duḥkhinaḥ devāḥ bhrātṛ bhāvāt muni īśvara duḥkhitāḥ te surāḥ sarve śivam śaraṇam ā yayuḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ bhagavaṃtam maheśvaram āhūya sa mahādevaḥ bhaktānām sarva kāma daḥ nāradam prerayāmāsa deva kārya cikīrṣayā atha deva muniḥ jñānī śaṃbhu bhaktaḥ satām gatiḥ śiva ājñayā yayau daitya pure devān sa nāradaḥ vyākulāḥ te surām sarve vāsava ādyāḥ drutam munim nāradāya surāḥ śakra mukhāḥ utkaṃṭhita ānanāḥ punar procuḥ surāḥ dīnāḥ vāsava ādyā sunīśvaram devāḥ ūcuḥ bho bho muni vara śreṣṭha duḥkham śṛṇu kṛpā kara śrutvā tat nāśaya kṣipram prabhuḥ tvam śaṃkara priyaḥ jalaṃdhareṇa daityena surāḥ vidrāvitāḥ bhṛśam sva sthānāt bhartṛ bhāvāt ca duḥkhitāḥ vayam ākulāḥ sva sthānāt uṣṇaraśmiḥ ca candraḥ nissāritaḥ tathā su baliṣṭhena vai tena sarve devāḥ prapīḍitāḥ duḥkham prāptāḥ vayam ca ati śaraṇam tvām samāgatāḥ saṃgrāme sa hṛṣīkeśam sva vaśam kṛtavān valī tasya vaśyaḥ vara adhīnaḥ avātsīt tad sadane hariḥ sa lakṣmyā sahitaḥ viṣṇu yoṃ naḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ jalaṃdhara vināśāya yatnam kuru mahāmate tvam naḥ daiva vaśāt prāptaḥ sadā sarva artha sādhakaḥ iti ākarṇya vacaḥ teṣām amarāṇām sa nāradaḥ āśvāsya muni śārdūlaḥ tān uvāca kṛpā karaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca jāne aham surāḥ yūyam daitya rāja parājitāḥ duḥkham prāptāḥ pīḍitāḥ ca sthānāt nissāritāḥ khalu sva śaktyā bhavatām sva artham kariṣye na atra saṃśayaḥ anukūlaḥ aham iha vaḥ duḥkham prāptāḥ yatas amarāḥ evam uktvā muni śreṣṭha draṣṭum dānava vallabham āśvāsya sakalān devān jalaṃghara sabhām yayau atha āgatam muni śreṣṭham dṛṣṭvā devaḥ jalaṃdharaḥ utthāya parayā bhaktyā dadau śreṣṭha āsanam varam kutas āgamyate brahman ki ca dṛṣṭam tvayā kacid yad artham iha āyātaḥ tat ājñāpaya mām mune jalaṃghūram nāradaḥ uvāca gataḥ kailāsa śikharam daitya indra aham yadṛcchayā kāmadhenu śata ākīrṇe ciṃtāmaṇi su dīpitam tatra umayā saha āsīnam dṛṣṭavān asmi śaṃkaram tam dṛṣṭvā mahat āśca me abhavat tadā kā api īdṛśī bhavet vṛddhiḥ trailokye vā navā iti caṃ tāvat ttava api daitya indra samṛddhiḥ saṃsmṛtā mayā tad vilokana kāmaḥ aham tvad sāṃnidhyam iha āgataḥ sva samṛddhim samayām vai darśayāmāsa sādaram dṛṣṭvā sa nāradaḥ jñānī deva kārya su sādhakaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca maṇayaḥ ratna puṃjāḥ ca gaja ādya aśva samṛddhayaḥ te gṛhe adya vibhānti iha yāni ratnāni tāni api tvayā śakrasya airāvataḥ tathā aśva ratnam mahāvīra sūryaḥ sya uccaiḥśravāḥ hayaḥ haṃsa yukta vimānam ca tvayā nītam hi vedhasaḥ iti evam vara ratnāni divi pṛthvyām rasātale yāni daitya indra te bhānti gṛhe tāni samastatas tvad samṛddhim imām paśyan sampūrṇī vividhām aham prasannaḥ asmi mahā vīra gaja aśva ādi su śobhitām jāyā ratnam mahā śreṣṭham jalaṃdhara na te gṛhe tat ānetum viśeṣeṇa strī ratnam vai tvam arhasi jāyā ratnam na ced tāni na śobhate vṛthā dhruvam iti evam vacanam śrutvā nāradasya mahātmanaḥ tadā āneṣye tatas brahman satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca tasya bhāryā su ramyā sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitā sarvāṃgasundarī nāmnā pāvatī iti manoharā tat īdṛśam rūpam ananya saṃgatam dṛṣṭam na kutra api kutūhala āḍhyam jāyā ratna anvitāt vīra trilokyām na jalaṃdhara yasyāḥ lāvaṇya jaladhau nimagna śvatura ānanaḥ nija taṃtraḥ api hi yatas sa sva ātma vaśagaḥ kṛtaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudra saṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdhara vadha upākhyāne devarṣi jalaṃdharasaṃvādaḥ nāma aṣṭadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca daitya rāj kim akārṣīt sa tat me vada su vistarāt tad rūpa śravaṇāt āsīt anaṃga jvara pīḍitaḥ atho jalaṃdharaḥ daityaḥ kāla adhīnaḥ pranaṣṭa dhīḥ dūtam āhvāyayāmāsa saiṃhikeyam vimohitaḥ āgatam tam samālokya kāma ākrāṃta manāḥ sa hi su saṃvodhya samācaṣṭa siṃdhu putraḥ jalaṃdharaḥ bho bho dūṃtavara śreṣṭha sarva kārya prasādhaka saiṃhikeya mahā prājña kailāsam gaccham parvatam tatra asti yogī śabhva ākhyaḥ tapasvī ca jaṭādharaḥ jaṭā dharam viraktam tam nirbhayena hṛdā tvayā mad nāthe bhuvane yogin na ucitā gatiḥ īdṛśī balāt gṛhītam sahasā pārijātaḥ taruḥ tathā vimānam haṃsa saṃyuktam aṃgaṇe mama tiṣṭhati chatram me vāruṇam gehe kāṃcanatrāvi tiṣṭhati mahāmālā sarvadā mlāna paṃkajā mad pituḥ sā mama eva asti pāśaḥ ca ke pateḥ tathā mṛtyoḥ utkrāṃti dā śaktiḥ mayā nītā valāt varā dadau mahyam śuciḥ divye śuci śauce ca vāsasī evam yogi indra ratnāni sarvāṇi vilasaṃti me tatra gatvā śivam sākṣāt devadevam mahā prabhum mahā rāja upacāreṇa vilasaṃtam mahā adbhutam sarva aṅga sundaram divya bhūṣaṇaiḥ bhūṣitam haram praṇanāma ca tam garvāt tat tejaḥ krāṃta vigrahaḥ nikaṭam gataṃvān śaṃbhoḥ sa dūtaḥ rāhu saṃjñakaḥ tryaṃbakam sa tadā saṃjñā preritaḥ vākyam abravīt dūtaḥ aham preṣitaḥ tena tvad sakāśam iha āgataḥ rāhuḥ uvāca svaḥ jñātau ātmani svam triṣu ātmīye svaḥ astriyām dhane iti amaraḥ sa daitya rājaḥ balavān devānām aṃtakaḥ umamaḥ yoginam tvā samuddiśya sa yat āha śṛṇuṣva tat sarva ratna īśvarasya tvam ājñām śṛṇu vṛṣadhvaja śmaśāna vāsinaḥ nitya masthi mālā dharasya ca digaṃbarasya te bhāryā katham haimavatī śubhā aham ratna adhināthaḥ asmi sā ca strī ratna saṃjñitām tasmāt mama eva sā yogyā na eva bhikṣā āśinaḥ tava mama vaśyāḥ trayaḥ lokāḥ muṃje aham makha bhāgakān sva strī ratnam dehi mahyam rājñaḥ sukha karāḥ prajāḥ dadati evam tathā rāhau bhrū madhyāt śūlapāṇinaḥ urddha keśaḥ śuṣka tanu nṛ siṃhaḥ iva ca aparaḥ mahā tanuḥ mahā vāhuḥ tāla jaṃghaḥ bhayaṃkaraḥ sa tam khāditum āyāntam dṛṣṭvā arāhuḥ bhaya āturaḥ rāhuḥ uvāca devadeva maheśāna pāhi mām śaraṇa āgatam brāhmaṇam mām mahādeva khāditum samupāgataḥ puruṣaḥ ayam tava īśāna sevaka ūti bhayaṃkaraḥ etasmāt rakṣa deveśa śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ na khādeta yathā ayam mām namaḥ te tu muhur muhur mahādevaḥ vacaḥ śrutvā brāhmaṇasya tadā mune abravīt sva gaṇam tam vai dīna anātha priyaḥ prabhuḥ mahādevaḥ uvāṃca prabhum ca brāhmaṇam dūtam rāhra ākhyam śaraṇa āgatam śaraṇyā rakṣaṇīyā hina daṇḍayā gaṇa sattama iti uktau girijā īśena sa gaṇaḥ karuṇā tmanā rāhum tatyājam sahasā brāhmaṇa iti śruta akṣaraḥ rāhum tyaktvā ambare saḥ utha puruṣaḥ dīnayā girā śiva upakaṃṭham āgatya mahādevam vyajijñapat puruṣaḥ uvāca devadeva mahādeva karuṇākara śaṃkara tyājitam mama bhakṣyam te śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ kṣudhā mām bādhate svāmin kṣudh kṣāmaḥ ca asmi kim bhakṣyam mama deveśa tat ājñāpaya mām prabho bubhukṣā yadi te atīva kṣudhā tvām bādhate yadi saṃbhakṣaya ātmanaḥ śīghram māṃsam tvam hasta pādayoḥ sa śivena evam ājñapta śvakhāda puruṣaḥ svakam hasta pāda udbhavam māṃsam śiraḥ śeṣaḥ abhavat yathā dṛṣṭvā śiraḥ vaśeṣam tu su prasannaḥ sadāśivaḥ puruṣam bhīma karmāṇam samuvāca sa vismayaḥ śivaḥ uvāca he mahā gaṇa dhanyaḥ tvam mad ājñā pratipālakaḥ saṃtuṣṭa śvā asmi num ārṣaḥ mahā gaṇaḥ mahā vīraḥ sarva duṣṭa bhayaṃkaraḥ mad priyaḥ tvam mada cā yām sadā pūjyaḥ ahi majjanaiḥ iti śaṃbho varam prāpya puruṣaḥ prajaharṣa saḥ tadā prabhṛti deveśa dvāre kīrtimukhaḥ sthitaḥ pūjanīyaḥ viśeṣeṇa sa gaṇaḥ śśiva pūjane na arcayanti iha ye pūrvam teṣām arcā vṛthā bhavet itiṃ śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudra saṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe dūtasaṃvādaḥ nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sana tkumāra sarvajña kathā te śrāvitā adbhutā mahā prabhoḥ śaṃkarasya yatra līlā ca pāvanī idānīm brūhi su prītyā kṛpām kṛtvā mama upari rāhuḥ muktaḥ kutra gataḥ puruṣeṇa mahā mune sūtaḥ uvāca gata garvaḥ jaṃgāma atha jalaṃdhara puram śanais jalaṃdharāya saḥ abhyetya sarvam īśa viceṣṭitam kathayāmāsa tad vayāsāt vayāsam daitya īśvarāya vai udyogam sarva sainyānām daityānām ādideśa ha nirgacchantu akhilāḥ daityāḥ kālanemi mukhāḥ khalu tathā śuṃbha niśuṃbha ādyāḥ vīrāḥ sva bala saṃyutāḥ koṭi vara kula utpannāḥ kaṃbu vaṃśya aśva daurhṛdāḥ kālakāḥ kālakeyāḥ ca mauryāḥ dhaumrāḥ tathā eva ca iti ājñāpya asura patiḥ sidhu putraḥ pratāpavān nirjagāma āśu daityānām koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ tatas rāhuḥ chinna śiraḥ abhavat vyarājata namaḥ pūrṇa prāvṛṣi iva yathā ghanaiḥ jātāḥ a śakunāḥ bhūri mahā nidrā visūcakāḥ tasya udyogam tathā dṛṣṭvā gīrvāṇāḥ te sa vāsavāḥ alakṣitāḥ tadā jagmuḥ kailāsam śaṃkara ālayam tatra gatvā śivam dṛṣṭvā su praṇamya sa vāsavāḥ devāḥ sarve na ta skaṃdhāḥ karau baddhā ca tuṣṭuvuḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ śaṃkara namaḥ te tu maheśāna pāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān upadravāt sa deva indrāḥ sthāna bhraṣṭāḥ jhiṃti sthitāḥ na jānāsi katham svāmin deva āpattim imām prabho tasmāt naḥ rakṣaṇa arthāya jahi sāgaranandanam asmākam rakṣaṇa arthāya yat pūrvam garuḍa dhvajaḥ vayam ca tatra tiṣṭhāmaḥ tad ājñā vaśagā ssurāḥ alakṣitāḥ vayam ca atra āgatāḥ śaṃbho tvad aṃtikam saḥ āyāti tvayā karttum raṇam siṃdhusutaḥ balī hetum arhasi sarvajña pāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān iti uktvā te surāḥ sarve prabhum natvā sa vāsavāḥ pādau nirīkṣya saṃtasthuḥ maheśasya vinamrakāḥ iti deva vacaḥ śrutvā prahasya vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ drutam viṣṇum samāhūya vacanam ca idam abravīt īśvaraḥ uvāca hṛṣīkeśa mahā viṣṇo devāḥ ca atra samāgatāḥ jalaṃdhara kṛta āpīḍāḥ śaraṇam me ati vihvalāḥ jalam dharaḥ katham viṣṇo saṃgare na hataḥ tvayā tad gṛham ca api yātaḥ asi tyaktvā vaikuṃṭham ātmanaḥ mayā niyojitaḥ tvam hi sādhu saṃrakṣaṇāya ca nigrahāya khalānām ca svataṃtreṇa vihāriṇā iti ākarṇya maheśaṃsya vacanam garuḍadhvajaḥ pratyuvāca vinīta ātmā natakaḥ saḥ aliḥ hariḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca tava aṃśa saṃbhava tvāt ca bhrātṛ tvāt ca tathā śriyaḥ mahā balaḥ mahāvīraḥ jeya anyeṣām ca api deveśa satyam etat ravīmi aham tvad parākramataḥ tuṣṭaḥ varam brūhi iti aham khalu mada dhīnaḥ mahāviṣṇo iti aham tad gṛham gataḥ iti viṣṇoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā śaṃkaraḥ sa maheśvaraḥ he viṣṇo sura varya tvam śṛṇu mad vākyam ādarāt jalaṃdharam mahā daityam iniṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ nirbhayāḥ vīta saṃdehāḥ hatam matvā surādhipam iti śrutvā maheśasya vacanam sa ramāpatiḥ sa nirjaraḥ jagāma āśu sva sthānam gata saṃśayaḥ sannadaiḥ asuraiḥ sārddham śaila prāṃtam yayau balī saṃtasthau kāla saṃkāśaḥ kurvan siha ravam mahān cukrodha ati mahā īśānaḥ mahā līlaḥ khala aṃtakaḥ samādideśa saṃkhyāya sva gaṇān sa mahā balān naṃdi ādikān mahādevaḥ mahā ūtiḥ kautukī haraḥ nandi ibha mukha senā nī mukhāḥ sarve śiva ājñayā gaṇāḥ ca samanahyanta yuddhāya ati tvarā anvitāḥ ava teruḥ gaṇāḥ sarve kailāsāt krodha durmadāḥ balgataḥ raṇa śabdān ca mahā vīrāḥ raṇāya hi pramatha adhipa daityānām ghoram śastra astra saṃkulam bherī mṛdaṃga śaṃkha odhaiḥ nissvāna evara harṣaṇaiḥ gaja aśva ratha śabdaiḥ ca nāditā bhūḥ vyakaṃpata vyarājata nabhaḥ pūrṇa muktābhiḥ iva saṃvṛtam vajra āhataiḥ parvata indraiḥ pūrvam āsīt su saṃvṛtā vasā asṛj māṃsa kāḍhyā bhūḥ agamyā bhavat tadā yuddhe punar punar ca eva mṛta saṃjīvanī balāt dṛṣṭvā vyākulitān tān tu gaṇāḥ sarve bhaya arditāḥ śaśaṃsuḥ devadevāya sarve śuka viceṣṭitam atha rudra mukhāt kṛtyā vabhūva ata vibhīṣaṇā tāla jaṃghā darī iva kā stana āpīḍita bhūruhā vicacāra mahā bhīmā bhakṣayaṃtī mahā asurān sva tejasā na bho vyāpya bhūmim kṛtvā ca sā mune bhārgavam sva bhage dhṛtvā jagāma aṃtarhitā nabhaḥ vidhṛtam bhārgavam dṛṣṭvā daitya sainya gaṇāḥ tathā daityānām senā gaṇa bhaya arditā vāyu vega hatā yadvat prakīrṇā tṛṇa saṃhatiḥ bhagnām gaṇa bhayāt daitya senām dṛṣṭvā ati marṣitāḥ niśuṃbha śubhau senānyau kālanemiḥ ca cukudhuḥ trayaḥ te vārayāmāsuḥ gaṇa senām mahā balāḥ mrucantaḥ śara varṣāṇi prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ tatas daitya śara oghāḥ te śalabhānām iva vrajāḥ rurudhuḥ kham diśaḥ sarvāḥ gaṇa senām akaṃpayan gaṇāḥ śara śataiḥ bhinnāḥ rudhira āsāra varṣiṇaḥ vasaṃta kiṃśuka ābhāsāḥ na prājāna nhi kiṃcana tvarā anvitāḥ daitya varān prasahya nivārayāmāsuḥ amarṣaṇāḥ te iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdharavadhopākhyāne sāmānyagaṇāsurayuddhavarṇanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ te gaṇa adhipatīn dṛṣṭvā nandi ibha sukha ṣaṇmukhān amarṣāt abhyadhāvanta dvaṃdva yuddhāya dānavāḥ nandinam kālanemiḥ ca śuṃbhaḥ laṃbodaram tathā niśuṃbhaḥ ṣaṇmukham devam abhyadhāvata śaṃkitaḥ niśuṃbhaḥ kārtikeyasya mayūram paṃcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śakti dharaḥ kruddhaḥ bāṇaiḥ paṃcabhiḥ eva ca śareṇa anyena tīkṣṇena niśuṃbham deva vairiṇam asuraḥ api niśuṃbha ākhyaḥ mahā vīraḥ ati vīryavān jaghāna kārtikeyam tam garjatam sva iṣuṇā raṇe tatas śaktim kārtikeyaḥ yāvat jagrāha roṣataḥ tāvat niśuṃbhaḥ vegena sva śaktyā tam apātayat evam babhūva tatra eva kārtikeya niśuṃbhayoḥ āhavaḥ hi mahān vyāsa vīra śabdam pragarjatoḥ tatas nandīśvaraḥ bāṇaiḥ kālanemim avidhyata saptabhiḥ ca hayān ketum ratham daḥ naṃdinaḥ sva śarāsana āniyuktaiḥ mahā tīkṣṇaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ atha nandīśvaraḥ vīraḥ kālanemim mahā asuram tam apāsya ca śūlena vakṣasi abhyahanam dṛḍham sa śūla bhinna hṛdayaḥ hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ adreḥ śikharam utpāṭya nandinam samatāḍayat atha śuṃbhaḥ gaṇeśaḥ ca ratha mūṣaka vāhanau gaṇeśaḥ tu tadā śubham hṛdi vivyādha patriṇā sārathim ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pātayāmāsa bhū tale tatas ati kruddha śśuṃbhaḥ api bāṇa vṛṣṭayā gaṇādhipam mūṣakam ca tribhiḥ viddhā nanāda jalada svanaḥ mūṣakaḥ śara bhinna aṅga śvacāla dṛḍha vedanaḥ tatas lambodaraḥ śuṃbham hatvā paraśunā hṛdi apātayat tadā bhūmau mūṣakam ca āruroha saḥ kālanemiḥ niśuṃbha śva śubhau laṃbodaram śaraiḥ yugapad cakhnatuḥ krodhāt āśī viṣa samaiḥ hatam tam pīḍyamānam ālokya vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ kūṣmāṃḍāḥ bhairavāḥ ca api vetālāḥ yoginī gaṇāḥ piśācāḥ ḍākinī saṃghāḥ gaṇāḥ ca api samam yayuḥ vināditā ḍamarukaiḥ pṛthivī samakaṃpata tatas bhūtāḥ pradhāvataḥ bhakṣayati sma dānavān utpatya pātayaṃti sma nanṛtuḥ ca raṇa aṃgaṇe etasmin atare vyāsa abhūtām nandī guhaḥ ca tau utthita avāpta saṃjñau hi jagarjatuḥ alam raṇe sa nandī kārtikeyaḥ ca samāyātau tvarā anvitau jannatuḥ ca raṇe daityāḥ niraṃtara śara vrajaiḥ vyākulā sā abhavat senā viṣaṇṇa vadanā tadā evam nandī kārtikeyaḥ vikaṭaḥ ca pratāpavān kālanemiḥ mahā daityaḥ asurāḥ ca anye parājitāḥ pravidhvastām tatas senām dṛṣṭvā sāgara nandanaḥ tatas parājitāḥ daityāḥ api abhūvan mahā utsavāḥ sarve rudra gaṇāḥ ca api jagarjuḥ jaya śālinaḥ hasti aśva ratha saṃhrādaḥ śaṃkha bherī ravaḥ tathā śailādi paṃcabhiḥ viddhāḥ gaṇeśa paṃcabhiḥ śaraiḥ śap ḻuk abhāvaḥ ārṣaḥ vīrabhadram ca viṃśatyā nanāda jalada svanaḥ jalaṃdharam mahā vīraḥ rudra putrāḥ nanāda ca papāta bhūmau tvaritam udatiṣṭhat mahā balaḥ tatas krodha parīta ātmā kārtikeyam jalaṃdharaḥ gadayā tāḍayāmāsa hṛdaye daitya puṃgavaḥ gadā prabhāvam saphalam darśayan śaṃkara ātmajaḥ tathā eva naṃdī hi apatat bhū tale gadayā hṛtaḥ mahāvīraḥ api ripu hā kiṃcid vayākula mānasaḥ tatas gaṇeśvaraḥ kruddhaḥ smṛtvā śiva pada ambu jam gaṇeśam pātayāmāsa ratham anyam samāruhat vigaṇayya hṛdā tam vai vīrabhadram ruṣā anvitaḥ vīrabhadram jaghāna āśu tīkṣṇena āśīviṣeṇa tam nanāda ca mahā vīraḥ daitya rājaḥ jalam gharaḥ vīrabhadraḥ api saṃkruddhaḥ sita dhāreṇa ca iṣuṇā nānā śastraiḥ tathā astraiḥ ca ciram vīra vara uttamau dhanuḥ ciccheda rathinaḥ patākām ca api vegataḥ vīrabhadra upakaṃṭham sa drutam āpa mahā balaḥ parighena ati mahatā vīrabhadram jaghāna haṃ parighena ati mahatā bhinna mūrddhā gaṇādhipaḥ patitam vīrabhadram tu dṛṣṭvā rudra gaṇāḥ bhayāt āpa agaccha traṇam hitvā krośamānā maheśvaram atha kolāhalam śrutvā gaṇānām candraśekharaḥ nija pārśva sthitān vīrān apṛcchat guṇa sattamān śaṃkaraḥ uvāca kimartham mad guṇānām hi mahā kolāhalaḥ abhavat vicāryatām mahāvīrāḥ śāṃtiḥ kāryā mayā dhruvam tāvat guṇa varāḥ te hi samāyātāḥ prabhum prati tān dṛṣṭvā vikalān nudraḥ papraccham kuśalam prabhuḥ yathāvat te gaṇāḥ vṛttam samācakhyuḥ ca vistarāt atra guṇa abhāvaḥ ārṣaḥ tat śrutvā bhagavān rudraḥ mahā līlā karaḥ prabhuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdhara upākhyāne viśeṣayuddhavarṇanam nāma ekaviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ abhyagāt ṛṣam ārūḍhaḥ saṃgrāmam prahasan iva rudra māyām tam ālokya siṃha nādaiḥ gaṇāḥ punar nivṛttāḥ saṃgareḥ raudrāḥ ye hi pūrva parājitāḥ vīra śabdam ca kurvantaḥ te api anye śāṃkarāḥ gaṇāḥ sa utsavāḥ sa āyudhāḥ daityān nijaghnuḥ śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ daityāḥ hi bhīṣaṇam rudram sarve dṛṣṭvā vidudruvuḥ śāṃkaram puruṣam dṛṣṭvā pātakāni iva tad bhayāt abhyadhāvat sa caṃḍīśam muṃcan bāṇān sahasraśas niśuṃbha śuṃbha pramukhāḥ daitya indrāḥ ca sahasraśas abhijagmuḥ śivam vegāt roṣāt saṃdaṣṭa dacchadāḥ kālanemiḥ tathā vīraḥ khaḍgaromā balāhakaḥ ghasmaraḥ ca pracaṃḍaḥ ca apare ca api śivam yayuḥ bāṇaiḥ saṃchādayāmāsuḥ hatam rudra gaṇān ca te aṃgāni cicchiduḥ vīrāḥ śuṃbha ādyāḥ nikhilāḥ mune bāṇa aṃdhakāra saṃchannam dṛṣṭvā gaṇa balam haraḥ tat vāṇa jālam ācchidya bāṇaiḥ āvavṛte namaḥ daityān ca vāṇa vātyābhiḥ pīḍitān akarot tadā pracaṃḍa bāṇa jāla oghaiḥ apātayata bhū tale khaṃḍga roma śiraḥ kāyāt tathā paraśunā ācchinat balāhakasya ca śiraḥ khaḍḍāṃgena akarot didhā mahā vīram ca cakartta triśikhena ha vṛṣabheṇa hatāḥ kecid kecid vāṇaiḥ nipātitāḥ na śekuḥ asurāḥ sthātum gaja ariṃsaha arditāḥ iva tatas krodha parīta ātmā daityān dhik kṛtavān raṇe śubha ādikān mahā daityaḥ prahasan prāha dhairyavān kim uccaritaiḥ mātuḥ ghāvadbhiḥ pṛṣṭhatas hataiḥ na hi bhīta vadhaḥ ślāghyaḥ svarga daḥ śūra māninām yadi vaḥ pradhane śraddhā sāraḥ vā kṣullakāḥ hṛdi agre tiṣṭhata mātram me na ced rāmya sukhe spṛhā raṇe mṛtyuḥ vara śvā asti sarva kāma phala pradaḥ yaśaḥ pradaḥ viśeṣeṇa mokṣa daḥ api prakīrttitaḥ sūryasya maṃḍalam bhittvā yāyāt vaiḥ paramam padam parivāda parama jñānī raṇe yaḥ saṃmukhe hataḥ mṛtyuḥ janmavatām vīrāḥ dehena saha jāyate adya vā abda śata aṃte vā mṛtyuḥ vai prāṇinām dhruvaḥ sarvathā parama ānandaḥ iha amutra api asaṃśayaḥ atha dṛṣṭvā sva sainyam tat palāyana parāyaṇam tatas yuṣmābhiḥ iti arthe vasā ādeśam ārṣaḥ krodhāt udam jalaṃdharaḥ āhvāpayāmāsa raṇe tīvra aśani sama svanaḥ iti uktvā bāṇa saptatyā jaghāna vṛṣabhadhvajam jalaṃdharaḥ mahā daityaḥ śaṃbhum akkiṣṭa kāriṇam tān aprāptān mahādevaḥ jalaṃdhara śarān drutam prabhuḥ gadām ca tad kṣiptām sahasā eva maheśvaraḥ pārāśaryya mahā līlaḥ drutam bāṇaiḥ dvidhā akarot tathā api muṣṭim udyamya mahā kruddhaḥ mahā asuraḥ abhyudyayau mahā vegānam tam tad jighāṃsayā tāvat eva īśvareṇa āśu bāṇa oghaiḥ sa jalaṃdharaḥ akliṣṭa karmakāreṇa krośa mātra m apākṛtaḥ sasarja māyām gāṃdharvīm adbhutām rudra mohinīm tasya māyā prabhāvāt tu gaṃdharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ tatas nanṛtuḥ gaṃdhavā apsarasām gaṇāḥ tāla veṇu mṛdaṃgān ca vādayanti sma ca apare tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam gaṇaiḥ rudraḥ vimohitaḥ ekāgrībhūtam ā lokya rudram daityaḥ jalaṃdharaḥ kāmataḥ sa jagāma āśu yatra gaurī sthitā abhavat yuddhe śuṃbha niśuṃbha ākhyau sthāpayitvā mahā balau paṃcāsyaḥ trinetraḥ ca jaṭādharaḥ mahā vṛṣabham ārūḍhaḥ sarvathā rudra saṃnibhaḥ āsuyya māyayā vyāsa sa babhūva jalaṃdharaḥ atha rudram samāyāntam ālokya bhava valabhā yāvat dadarśa ca avaigīm pārvatīm danuja īśvaraḥ tāvat sa vīrya mumuce jaḍa aṃga vā abhavat tadā atha jñātvā tadā gaurī dānavam bhaya vihvalā jagāma aṃtarhitā vegāt sā tadā uttara mānasam tām adṛśya tatas daityaḥ kṣaṇāḥ dvi dyut latām iva pārvatī api mahā viṣṇum sasmāra manasā tadā tāvat dadarśa tam devam sa upaviṣṭam samīpa gam tam dṛṣṭvā pārvatī viṣṇum jaganmātā śivapriyā prasanna manasā uvāca praṇamatam kṛtāṃjalim pārvatī uvāca viṣṇo jalaṃdharaḥ daityaḥ kṛta vān parama adbhutam pratyuvāca śivām natvā sa aṃjaliḥ namra kaṃdharaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca bhavatyāḥ kṛpayā devi tat vṛttam viditam mayā yat ājñāpaya mām mātar tat kuryyām tvad anujñayā tat śrutvā viṣṇu vacanam punar api āha pārvatī hṛṣīkeśam jaganmātrī dharma nītim suśikṣayan tad strī pātitratam dharmam bhraṣṭam kuru mad ājñayā iti anujñām samākarṇya śirasā ādhāya tām hariḥ chalam karttum jagāma āśu punar jālaṃdharam puram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudra saṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdharavadhopākhyāne jalaṃdharayuddhavarṇanam nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca pātivratyasya bhaṃgāya vṛndāyāḥ ca akarot matim vṛdām sa darśayāmāsa svanam māyāvinām varaḥ atha vṛndā tadā devī tad patnī niśi suvratā hareḥ māyā prabhāvāt tu dussvapnam sā dadarśa ha svapna madhye hi sā viṣṇu māyayā pradadarśa ha bharttāram mahipa ārūḍham taila abhyaktam diś aṃbaram kṛṣṇa prasūna bhūṣā āḍhyam kravyāda gaṇa sevitam dakṣiṇa āśām gatam muṃḍam tamasā ca vṛtam tadā tatas prabudhya sā bālā tam svanam svam vicinvatī dadaśa uditam ādityam sa chidram niḥprabham muhur tat aniṣṭam idam jñātvā rudaṃtī bhaya vihvalā kutracid nā āpa sā śarma gopura aṭṭāla bhūmiṣu tatra api sā gatā bālā na prāpa kutracid sukham tatas jalaṃdhara strī sā nirviṇṇa udvigna mānasā vanāt vai na antaram yātā nā eva veda ātmanā tadā bhramatī sā tatas vālā dadarśa atīva bhīṣaṇau rākṣasau siṃha vadanau dṛṣṭvā daśana bhāsurau tau dṛṣṭvā lātī iva palāyana parā tadā dadarśa tāpasam śatim sa śiṣyam maunam āsthitam tatas tad kaṃṭham āsādya nija bāhu latām bhayāt sune mām rakṣa śaraṇam āgatā asi iti abhāṣata muniḥ tām vihvalām dṛṣṭvā rākṣasa anugatām tadā tanuṃkāra bhayam trastau dṛṣṭvā vimukhau gatau vismitā atīva daitya indra patnī sā abhūt mune hṛdi tatas sā suninātham tam bhayāt muktā kṛtāṃjaliḥ praṇamya daṃḍa vat bhūmau vṛndā vacanam atravīt vṛndā uvāca muninātha dayā sindho para pīḍā nivāraka rakṣitā aham tvayā ghorāt bhayāt asmāt khala udbhavāt kiṃcid vijñaptum icchāmi kṛpayā tat niśāmaya muniḥ tad vākyam ākarṇya maunam kapaṭam āsthitaḥ karttum sva artha vidhāna jñaḥ kṣata tāvat kapi īśau āyātau tam praṇamya agratas sthitau nītvā kṣaṇa arddham āgatya punar tasyāḥ tasya eva kam kabaṃdham ca hastau āstām muni īśvara śiraḥ kabaṃdham hastau tau dṛṣṭvā abdhi tanayasya sā papāta mūrcchitā bhūmau bhartṛ vyasana duḥkhitāḥ vṛndā uvāca yaḥ purā sukha saṃvādeḥ vinodayasi mām prabho yena devāḥ sa gaṃdharvāḥ nirjitāḥ viṣṇunā saha na aṃgīkṛtam hi me vākyam rudva tattvam a jānatā tatas tvam hi mayā jñātaḥ tava sevā prabhāvataḥ vilalāpa vicitram sā hṛdayena vidūyatā tatas sā dhairyam ālaṃbya duḥkha ucchvāsān vimuṃcatī uvāca muni varyai tam su praṇamya kṛtāṃjaliḥ vṛndā uvāca kṛpā nidhe su niśreṣṭha para upakaraṇa ādara mayi kṛtvā kṛpām sādho jīvaya enam mama prabhum atas saṃjīvaya enam me prāṇanātham muni īśvara iti uktvā daitya patnī sā pātivratya parāyaṇā pādayoḥ patitā tasya duḥkha śvāsān vimuñcatī na ayam jīvayitum śaktaḥ rudreṇa nihataḥ yudhi tathā api kṛpayā viṣṭaḥ enam saṃjīvayāmi aham rakṣyāḥ śaraṇa gāḥ ca iti jānan dharma sanātanam aṃtardadhe tatas viṣṇuḥ sarva māyāvinām varaḥ vṛndāḥ mā āliṃgya tad vakram cucumba prīta mānasaḥ atha vṛndā api bhartāram dṛṣṭvā harṣita mānasā atha prasanna hṛdayā sā hi saṃjāta hṛcchayā kadācid suratasyām dṛṣṭvā viṣṇum tam eva hi vṛndā uvāca dhik tat evam hare śīlam para dāra abhigāminaḥ jñātaḥ asi tvam mayā samyak māyī pratyakṣa tāpasaḥ śaśāpa keśavam vyāsa pātivratya ratā ca sā gṛhṇīṣva śaṭha mad dattam śāpam sarva viṣa ulbaṇam yau tvayā māyayā khyātau svakīyā ūm darśitaḥ mama tau eva rākṣasau bhūtvā bhāryau tava hari syataḥ tvam ca api vane kapi sahāyavān bhrama sapa iṃśvareṇa ayam yaḥ te śiṣya tvam āgataḥ iti uktvā sā tadā vṛndā prāviśat havyavāhanam viṣṇunā vāryamāṇā api tad smita āsakta cetasā āgatāḥ khe samam dāraiḥ sat gatim vai didṛkṣavaḥ paśyatām sarva devānām alokam agam adbhutam śivā tanau vilīnam tad vṛndā tejaḥ babhūva ha āsīt jaya jaya ārāvaḥ kha sthita amara paṃktiṣu evam vṛndā mahā rājñī kālanemi sutā uttamā pātivratya prabhāvāt ca muktim prāpa parām mune iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudra saṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdhara vadha upākhyāne vṛndāpatitratabhaṃgadehatyāgavarṇanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ a dhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca vidheḥ śreṣṭha prājña kathā iyam śrāvitā adbhutā a dṛśya girijām tatra daitya indre raṇam āgate gāṃdharve ca vilīne hi caitanyaḥ abhūt vṛṣadhvajaḥ aṃtardhāna gatām māyām dṛṣṭvā buddhaḥ hi śaṃkaraḥ cukrodha atīva saṃhārī laukikīm gatim āśritaḥ tatas śivaḥ vismita mānasaḥ punar jagāma yuddhāya jalaṃdharam ruṣā sa ca api daityaḥ punar āgatam śivam dṛṣṭvā śara oghaiḥ samavākirat raṇe kṣiptam prabhuḥ tam śara jāla mutram jalaṃdhareṇa ati balīyasā haraḥ cakāra māyayā gaurīm tryambakam mohayan iva ratha upari gatām baddhām rudatīm pārvatīm śivaḥ niśuṃbha śuṃbha daityaiḥ ca vadhyamānām dadarśa saḥ gaurīm tathāvidhām dṛṣṭvā laukikīm darśayan gatim babhūva prākṛtaḥ iva śivaḥ api udvigna mānasaḥ āvāṅmukha sthitaḥ tūṣṇīm nānā līlā viśāradaḥ śithila aṃgaḥ viṣaṇṇa ātmā vismṛtya sva parākramam tatas rudraḥ mahā līlaḥ jñāna tattvaḥ kṣaṇāt prabhuḥ raudra rūpa dharaḥ jātaḥ jvālā mālā ati bhīṣaṇaḥ tasya atīva mahā raudra rūpam dṛṣṭvā mahā asurāḥ na śekuḥ pramukhe sthātum bhejire te diśaḥ daśa niśuṃbha śubhau api yau vikhyātaḥ vīra sattamau api raṇe sthātum muni īśvara jalaṃdhara kṛtā māyā aṃtarhitā abhūt ca tad kṣaṇam hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt saṃgrāme sarvatomukhe tatas śāpam dadau rudraḥ tayoḥ śuṃbha niśuṃbhayoḥ palāyamānau tau dṛṣṭvā dhikkṛtya krodha saṃyutaḥ yuvām duṣṭau ati khalau aparādha karau mama pārvatī daṃḍa dātārau raṇā dasmāt parāṅmukhau mama yuddhāt atikrāṃtī gorkhāḥ vadhyau bhaviṣyataḥ rudre raṇe mahā vegāt vavarṣa niśitān śarān bāṇa aṃdhakāra saṃchannam tathā bhūmi talam hi abhūt tāvat sa parigheṇa āśu jaghāna vṛṣabham balī vṛṣaḥ tena prahāreṇa parāvṛttaḥ raṇa aṃgaṇāt rudreṇa kṛṣyamāṇaḥ api na tasthau raṇa bhūmiṣu darśayāmāsa sarva dṛṣṭvā puras sthitam daityam meru kūṭam iva sthitam brahmaṇaḥ vacanam rakṣatrakṣakaḥ jagatām prabhuḥ kopam kṛtvā param śūlī pādāṃguṣṭena līlayā mahā aṃbhasi cakāra āśu rathāṃgam raudram adbhutam kṛtvā arṇava aṃbhasi śitam bhagavān rathāṅga smṛtvā jagatrayam anena hataḥ purāriḥ dakṣa andhaka anta ka puratraya yajñahaṃtā lokatraya aṃtaka karaḥ prahasan uvāca balavān yadi ca uddhartum tiṣṭhan yoddhum na ca anyathā pradahan iva cakṣurbhyām prāha ālokya sa śaṃkaram rekhām uddhṛtya hatvā ca sa gaṇam tvām hi śaṃkara hatvā lokān suraiḥ sādai sva bhāgam garuḍaḥ yathā haṃtum carācaram sarvam samarthaḥ aham sa vāsavam brahmā baliṣṭhaḥ sthāne me munibhiḥ sura puṃgavaiḥ indra agni yama vitteśa vāyu vārīśvara ādayaḥ na sehire yathā nāgāḥ gaṃdham pakṣipateḥ iva na labdham divi bhūmau ca vāhanam mamam śaṃkara samastān parvatān prāpya dharṣitāḥ ca gaṇeśvarāḥ giri indraḥ mandaraḥ śrīmān nīlaḥ meruḥ su śobhanaḥ dharṣitaḥ bāhu daṇḍena kaṇḍvā utsarpaṇāya me gaṃgā niruddhā bāhubhyām līlā artham himavat virau arīṇām mama bhṛtyaiḥ śva jayaḥ labdhaḥ divaukasām vaḍavāyāḥ mukham baddham gṛhītvā tām kareṇa tu tad kṣaṇāt eva sakalam ekārṇavam abhūt tadā airāvata ādayaḥ nāgāḥ kṣiptāḥ sindhu jala upari garuḍaḥ api mayā baddhaḥ nāgapāśena viṣṇunā urvaśī ādyāḥ mayā nītāḥ nāryaḥ kārā gṛha aṃtaram mām na jānāsi rudra tvam trailokya jaya kāriṇam iti uktvā atha mahādevam tadā vāridhi nandanaḥ tiraskṛtaḥ mahādevaḥ vacanaiḥ kaṭuka akṣaraiḥ sudarśana ākhyam yad cakram pāda aṃguṣṭha vinirmitam sudarśana ākhyam tat cakram cikṣepa bhagavān haraḥ koṭi sūrya pratīkāśam pralaya anala sannibham vinā api tad yogam tṛtīyā vṛddhaḥ yūnā ityādi nirdeśāt rathāt kāyaḥ papāta uya nādayan vasudhā talam śiraḥ śvāpya abdhiṃputrasya hāhākāraḥ mahān abhūt dvidhā papāta tad dehaḥ hi aṃjana adriḥ iva acalaḥ kuliśena yathā vārāṃnidhau giri varaḥ dvidhā tatas sama stā pṛthivī vikṛtā abhūt muni īśvara mahārauravam āsādya raktakuṃḍam abhūt iha jalaṃdharam hatam dṛṣṭvā deva gandharva pannagāḥ sarve prasanna tām yātāḥ deva siddha muni īśvarāḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭi prakurvāṇāḥ tat yaśaḥ jaguḥ uccakais deva aṃganāḥ mahā āmodān nanṛtuḥ premavi hvalāḥ diśaḥ praseduḥ sarvāḥ ca han te vṛndāpatau mune vavruḥ puṇya as mukha sparśāḥ vāyavaḥ trividhāḥ api candramāḥ śīta tām yātaḥ raviḥ tepe su tejasā agnayaḥ jajvaluḥ śāṃtāḥ babhūva avikṛtam nabhaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdhara vadhavarṇanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha brahma ādayaḥ devā sunayaḥ ca akhilāḥ tathā tuṣṭuvuḥ devadeveśam vāgbhiḥ iṣṭabhiḥ ānatāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ yathāmati mahātmānaḥ sarvam gāyaṃti sat yaśaḥ māhātmyam aṃti gūḍham te sahasravadana ādayaḥ sadā gāyaṃti su prītyā punaṃti sva giram hi te kṛpayā tava deveśa brahma jñānī bhaveḥ jaḍaḥ bhakti gamyaḥ sadā tvam vām iti vedāḥ bruvaṃti hi tvam vai dīna dayāluḥ ca sarvatra vyāpakaḥ sadā purā yadu patiḥ bhuktaḥ dāśārhaḥ siṃddhim āgataḥ tathā mitrasahaḥ rājā madayaṃtī ca tad priyā bhuktvā bhogān ca vividhān tu a dbhaktyā prāpa sat gatim gopīputraḥ śrīkaraḥ te lopa daśā kalyasya iti ya lopaḥ param sukham mahāvīra śiṣyaḥ prāpa paratra vai tvad bhakti vartinam mātrā jñāninam kṛpayā karoḥ candrāṃgadaḥ rāja putraḥ sīmaṃtinyā striyā saha vihāya sakalam duḥkham sukhī prāpa mahā gatim dvijaḥ maṃdara nāmā api veśyā gāmī khalaḥ adhamaḥ tvad bhaktām śiva saṃpūjya tayā saha gatim gataḥ tvad bhakta kṛpayā mātrā gatim ca paramām prabho śaṃvaraḥ śaṃkaraḥ bhaktaḥ citā bhasma dharaḥ sadā niyamāt bhasmanaḥ śaṃbho sva striyā te puram gataḥ sudharma śubhakarmā ṇau sadā rudra akṣa dhāriṇau tvad kṛpātaḥ ca tau mukkau āstām bhuktvā iha sat sukham pūrva janmani yau kīśa kukkuṭaḥ rudra bhūṣaṇau piṃgalā ca mahā nandā veśye dve tava bhaktitaḥ śāradā vipra tanayāḥ bāla vaidhavyam āgatā vaṃcukā tvad yaśaḥ śrutvā paramām gatim āyayau bhakti bhāvāt maheśāna dīna bandho kṛpā ālaya nirguṇaḥ triguṇa ādhāraḥ brahma viṣṇu hara ātmakaḥ nānā karma karaḥ nityam nirvikāraḥ akhila īśvaraḥ prasannaḥ bhava deveśa rakṣa smān sarvadā śiva tvad prajāḥ ca vayam nātha sadā tvad śaraṇam gatāḥ iti stutvā ca te devāḥ brahma ādyāḥ sa muni īśvarāḥ tūṣṇīm babhūvuḥ hi tadā śivān tri dvandva cetasaḥ atha śaṃsuḥ maheśānaḥ śrutvā deva stutim śubhām devāḥ sarve api muditāḥ brahma ādyāḥ hata śatravaḥ svam svam dhāma yayuḥ prītāḥ gāyataḥ śiva sat yaśaḥ deva stutiḥ iyam puṇyā sarva pāpa praṇāśinī sarva saukhya pradā nityam maheśa ānaṃda dāyinī yaḥ paṭhet pāṭhayet vā api iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe jalaṃdharavadhopākhyāne devastutivarṇanam nāma paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca ārṣaḥ ayam yat śrāvitā mahā divyā kathā iyam śāṃkarī śubhā idānīm brūhi su prītyā caritam vaiṣṇavam mune sa vṛndām mohayitvā tu kim akārṣīt kutas gataḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahā prājña śaiva pravara sattama vaiṣṇavam caritam śaṃbhu carita āḍhyam su nirmalam maunībhūteṣu deveṣu brahma ādiṣu maheśvaraḥ śaṃbhuḥ uvāca sukham āpuḥ na vā tātāḥ satyam brūta amarāḥ khalu atha brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ harṣāt utphulla locanāḥ praṇamya śirasā rudram śaśaṃsuḥ viṣṇu ceṣṭitam devāḥ ūcuḥ mahādeva tvayā deva rakṣitāḥ śatru jāt bhayāt vṛndā vimohitā nātha viṣṇunā hi nataḥ bhasmībhūtāḥ drutam vahnau paramām gatim āṃgatā vṛndā lāvaṇya saṃbhrāṃtaḥ viṣṇuḥ tiṣṭhati mohitaḥ tad citā bhasma saṃghārī tava māyāḥ vimohitaḥ kṛpām kuru maheśāna viṣṇum bodhaya bodhaya tvad adhīnam idam sarvam prākṛtam sacarācaram prati u vāca mahā līlaḥ svacchandaḥ tān kṛtāṃjalīn maheśaḥ uvāca he brahman he surāḥ sarve mad vākyam śṛṇuta ādarāt mohinī sarva lokānām mama māyā duratyayā tad adhīnam jagat sarvam yat deva asura mānuṣam tayā eva mohitaḥ viṣṇuḥ kāma adhīnaḥ bhavat hariḥ umā ākhyā sā mahādevī trideva jananī parā mūlaprakṛtiḥ ākhyātā surāmā girija ātmikā gacchadhvam śaraṇāḥ devāḥ viṣṇu moha apanuttaye śaraṇyām mohinīm māyām śiva ākhyām sarva kāma dām stutim kuruta tasyāḥ ca mad śateḥ toṣaṃkāriṇīm iti uktvā tān surān śaṃbhuḥ paṃca āsyaḥ bhagavān haraḥ devāḥ ca śāsanāt śaṃbhoḥ brahma ādyāḥ hi sa vāsavāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ yad icchayā viśva m idam bhava abhavau tanoti mūlaprakṛti natāḥ sma tām pāhi trayoviṃśa guṇān su śabditān jagatī aśeṣe samadhiṣṭhitā parā yad rūpa karmāṇi trayaḥ api te viduḥ na mūlaprakṛtim natāḥ sma tām yat bhakti yuktāḥ puruṣāḥ tu nityam dāridrya moha atyaya saṃbhava ādīn kuru kāryam mahādevi devānām naḥ para īśvari jalam dharasya śaṃbhoḥ ca raṇe kailāsa vāsinaḥ pravṛtte tad vadha arthāya gaurī śāsanataḥ śive vṛndā vimohitā devi viṣṇunā hi praya tnataḥ sva vṛṣāt tyājitā vanhau bhasmībhūtā gatim gatā giriśena kṛpām kṛtvā bhakta anugraha kāriṇā tad ājñayā vayam sarve śaraṇam te samāgatāḥ tvam hi śaṃbhuvām devi bhakta uddhāra parāyaṇau vṛndā lāvaṇya saṃbhrāṃtaḥ viṣṇuḥ tiṣṭhati tatra vai tad citā bhasma saṃdhārī jñāna bhraṣṭaḥ vimohitaḥ yathā sva lokam pāyāt sa su cittaḥ sura kārya kṛt dadṛśuḥ aṃgane tatra jvālā vyāpta digaṃtaram tad madhyāt bhāratīm sarve brahma ādya aśva sa vāsavāḥ amarāḥ śuśruvuḥ vyāsa kāmardāḥ vyoma cāriṇīm ākāśavāṇī uvāca aham eva tridhā bhinnā tiṣṭhāmi trividhaiḥ guṇaiḥ gaurī lakṣmīḥ surā jyotiḥ rajaḥ sattva tamaḥ guṇaiḥ tatra gacchata yūyam vai tāsām aṃtike ādarāt mad ājñayā prasannāḥ tāḥ vidhāsyate tad īpsitam śṛṇvatām iti tām vācam aṃtar ddhānim agāt mahaḥ devānām vismaya utphulla netrāṇām tat tadā mune tatas sarve api te devāḥ śrutvā tad vākyam ādarāt gaurīm lakṣmīm surām ca eva nemuḥ tad vākya coditāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahā bhaktyā devīḥ tāḥ sakalāḥ surāḥ nānāvidhāḥ bhiḥ vāgbhiḥ te brahma ādyāḥ nata mastakāḥ tatas aram vyāsa devyaḥ tāḥ āvirbhūtāḥ ca tad puras atha tāḥ amarāḥ dṛṣṭvā su prasannena cetasā tatas ca etāḥ surān dṛṣṭvā praṇatān bhakta vatsalāḥ devyaḥ ūcuḥ imāni taṃtra bījāni viṣṇuḥ yatra avatiṣṭhati nirvapadhvam tatas kāryam bhavatām siddhim eṣyati rudra viṣṇu vidhīnām hi śaktayaḥ triguṇa ātmikāḥ tatas tuṣṭāḥ surāḥ sarve brahmā ādyā śva sa vāsavāḥ tāni bījāni saṃgṛhya yayuḥ yatra hari sthitaḥ vṛnda ācitā bhūmi tale cikṣipuḥ tāni te surāḥ smṛtvā tāḥ saṃsthi tāḥ tatra śiva śaktyam śakāḥ mune dhātrī ca mālatī ca eva tulasī ca muni īśvara dhātryudbhavā smṛtā dhātrī mābhavā mālatī smṛtā gaurī bhavā ca tulasī tamaḥ sattva rajaḥ guṇāḥ viṣṇuḥ vanaspatīḥ dṛṣṭvā tadā strī rūpiṇīḥ mune udatiṣṭhat tadā tāsu rāga atiśaya vibhra svadharmāt satī tva rūpāt ya ṇ ārṣaḥ puṃstvam ārṣam māt dṛṣṭvā sa yācate mohāt kāma āsaktena cetasā tam ca api tulasī dhātrī rāgena eva avalokatām yat ca bījam purā lakṣmyā māyayā eva sama rpitam tasmāt tad udbhavā nārī tasmin īrṣyā parā abhavat atas sā varvarī iti ākhyām avāpa atīva garhitām tatas vismṛta duḥkhaḥ asau viṣṇuḥ tābhyām sadā eva tu kārtike māsi vipra indra dhātrī ca tulasī sadā sarva deva priyā jñeyā viṣṇoḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ tatra api tulasī dhanyā atīva śreṣṭhā mahā mune tyaktvā gaṇeśam sarveṣām prīti dā sarvakā madā vaikuṇṭha stham harim dṛṣṭvā brahma indra ādyāḥ ca te amarāḥ natvā stutvā mahā viṣṇum sva sva dhāmāni vai yayuḥ sukhī ca abhūt muni śreṣṭha pūrvavat saṃsmaran śivam iti ākhyānam aghas ghanam sarva kāma pradam nṛṇām yaḥ idam hi paṭhet nityam pāṭhayet vā api bhaktimān śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet vā api sa yāti paramām gatim paṭhitvā yaḥ idam dhīmān ākhyānam parama uttamam saṃgrāmam praviśet vīraḥ vijayī syāt na saṃśayaḥ viprāṇām brahma vidyā dam kṣatriyāṇām jaya pradam vaiśyānām sarva dhana dam śūdrāṇām sukha dam tu idam śaṃbhu bhakti pradam vyāsa sarveṣām pāpa nāśanam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudra saṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe jalaṃdhara vadha anantara devīstutiviṣṇu mohavidhvaṃsavarṇanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha anyat śaṃbhu caritam premataḥ śṛṇu vai sune yasya śravaṇa mātreṇa śiva bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā bhavet śaṃkhacūḍa abhidhaḥ vīraḥ dānavaḥ deva kaṃṭakaḥ yathā śivena nihataḥ raṇa mūrdhni triśūlataḥ tat śaṃbhu caritam divyam pavitram pāpa nāśanam śṛṇu vyāsa su saṃprītyā vacmi su snehataḥ tava marīceḥ tanayaḥ dhātuḥ putraḥ yaḥ kaśyapaḥ muniḥ sa dharmiṣṭhaḥ sṛṣṭi karttā vidhi ājñaptaḥ prajāpatiḥ tāsām prasūtiḥ prasabham na kathyā bahu vistṛtāḥ prastutam śṛṇu vṛttāṃtam śaṃbhu līlā anvitam ca yat tāsu kaśyapa patnīṣu danuḥ tu ekā vara aṃganā mahā rūpavatī sādhvī pati saubhāgya varddhitā āsaḥ tasyāḥ danoḥ putrāḥ bahavaḥ balavattarāḥ teṣām nāmāni nā ucyate vistāra bhayataḥ mune śukra ācārya gurum kṛtvā kṛṣṇa maṃtram avāpya ca tapaḥ cakāra paramam puṣkare lakṣa varṣakam kṛṣṇa maṃtram jajāpa eva dṛḍham vaddha āsanam ciram tapaḥ sunāsī puraskṛtya brahmāṇam śaraṇam yayuḥ praṇamya ca vidhātāram dātāram sarva saṃpadām tuṣṭuvuḥ vikalāḥ procuḥ sva vṛttāṃta viśeṣataḥ tat ākarṇya vidhā tāpi vaikuṃṭham taiḥ yayau saha tatra gatvā triloka īśam viṣṇum rakṣā karam param praṇamyam tuṣṭavaḥ sarve karau baddhāḥ vinamrakāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ devadeva na jānīmaḥ jātam kim kāraṇam tu iha saṃtaptāḥ sakalāḥ jātāḥ tejasām kena tat vada tapta ātmanām tvam avitā dīna baṃdhaḥ anujīvinām rakṣa rakṣa ramānātha śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān iti śrutvā vacaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahma ādīnām divaukasām uvāca vihasan premṇā śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca su svasthāḥ bhavata avyagrāḥ naḥ bhayam kuruta amarāḥ dānavaḥ daṃbha nāmā hi mad bhaktaḥ kurute tapaḥ putra arthī śamayiṣyāmi tam aham vara dānataḥ acyutaḥ api varam dātum puṣkaram saṃja gāma ha tapaḥ carati yatra asau daṃbha nāmā hi dānavaḥ tatra gatvā varam brūhi iti uvāca parisāṃtvayan girā sūnṛtayā bhaktam japatam sva manum hariḥ tat śrutvā vacanam viṣṇoḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ca pura sthitam praṇanāma mahā bhaktyā tuṣṭāva ca punar punar daṃbhaḥ uvāca ramānātha triloka īśa kṛpām kuru mama upari gate harau dānava indraḥ kṛtvā tasyai diśe namaḥ jagāma sva gṛham siddha tapāḥ pūrṇa manorathaḥ rarāja tejasā atyaṃtam rocayaṃtī gṛha aṃtaram sudāmā nāma gopaḥ yaḥ kṛṣṇasya pārṣadāgraṇīḥ tasyāḥ garbhe viveśa asau rādhā śaptaḥ ca yat mune asūta samaye sādhvī suprabham tanayam tatas jātakam sucakāra asau pitā āhūya munīn vahūn nāma cakre pitā tasya śaṃkhacūḍa iti sat dine sa śukla pakṣe yathā śaśī sa bāla krīḍayā nityam pitroḥ harṣam tatāna ha priyaḥ babhūva sarveṣām kula jānām viśeṣataḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām paṃcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍotpattivarṇanam nāma saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas ca śaṃkhacūḍaḥ asau jīgīṣavya upadeśataḥ tapaḥ cakāra su prītyā brahmaṇaḥ puṣkare ciram saḥ ekāgra manāḥ bhūtvā karaṇāni nigṛhya ca tapatam puṣkare tam vai śaṃkhacūḍam ca dānavam varam dātum jagama āśu brahmā lokaguruḥ vibhuḥ varam brūhi iti provāca dānava indram vidhiḥ tadā sa dṛṣṭvā tam nanāma atina mraḥ tuṣṭāva sat virā varam yayāce brahmāṇam ajeya tvam divaukasām śrī kṛṣṇa kavacam divyam jagat maṃgala maṃgalam dattavān śaṃkhacūḍāya sarvatra vijaya pradam badarīm saṃprayāhi tvam tulasyā saha tatra vai antardhānam jagāma āśu paśyataḥ tasya tad kṣaṇāt tatas sa śaṃkhacūḍaḥ hi tapaḥ siddhaḥ ati puṣkare ājñayā brahmaṇaḥ tapaḥ siddha manorathaḥ samāyayau prahṛṣṭa āsyaḥ tūrṇa badarikāśramam yadṛcchayā gataḥ tatra śaṃkhacūḍaḥ ca dānavaḥ tapaḥ carantī tulasī yatra dharmadhvaja ātmajā surūpā su smitā tanvī śubha bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitā sa kaṭākṣam dadarśa asau tam eva puruṣam param dṛṣṭvā tām lalitām ramyām su śīlām sundarīm satīm uvāsa tad samīpe tu madhuram tām uvāca saḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ uvāca kā tvam kasya sutā tvam hi kim karoṣi sthitā atra kim maunībhūtā kiṃkaram mām saṃbhāvitum iha arhasi iti evam vacanam śrutvā sa kāmam tam uvāca sā nārī jāti mohinī ca brahma ādīnām viṣa upamā nindyā doṣa karī māyā śrṛṃkhalā hi anuśāyinām dṛṣṭvā tām sa smitām saḥ upi pravaktum upacakrame śaṃkhacūḍaḥ uvāca kiñcid satya malīkam ca kiṃcid mattaḥ niśāmaya pativratāḥ striyaḥ yāḥ ca tāsām madhye tvam agraṇīḥ na ca aham pāpa dṛś kāmī tathā tvam na iti dhīḥ mama āgacchāmi tvad samīpam ājñayā brahmaṇaḥ adhunā gāṃdharveṇa vivāhena tvām grahīṣyāmi śobhane śaṃkhacūḍaḥ aham eva asmi deva vidrāva kārakaḥ mām na jānāsi kim bhadre na śrutaḥ aham kadācana danu vaṃśyaḥ viśeṣeṇa manda putraḥ ca dānavaḥ sudāmā nāma gopaḥ ūham pārṣadaḥ ca hareḥ purā adhunā dānava indraḥ aham rādhikāyāḥ ca śāpataḥ jātismaraḥ aham jānāmi sarve kṛṣṇa prabhāvataḥ evam uktvā śaṃkhacūḍa om virarāma ca tad puras dānava iṃdreṇa sā iti uktā vacanam satyam ādarāt tvayā aham adhunā sattvam vicāreṇa parājitā sa dhanyaḥ puruṣaḥ loke na striyā yaḥ parājitaḥ satkriyā upi aśuciḥ nityam saḥ pumān yaḥ striyā jitaḥ śudhyet vipraḥ daśa ahena jātake mṛta sūtake kṣatriyaḥ dvādaśa ahena vaiśyaḥ paṃcadaśa ahataḥ na śuciḥ strī jitaḥ kvāpi citā dāham vinā pumān na gṛhṇati icchayā tasmāt pitaraḥ piṃḍa tarpaṇam na gṛhṇāṃta sura stenam dattam puṣpa phala ādikam vidyā prabhāva jñāna artham mayā tvam ca parīkṣitaḥ kṛtvā kānta parīkṣām vai vṛṇuyāt kāminī varam iti evam pravadatyām tu tulasyām tad kṣaṇe vidhiḥ tatra ajāgama saṃsraṣṭā provāca vacanam tatas kim karoṣi śaṃkhacūḍa saṃvādam anayā saha gāṃdharveṇa vivāhena tvam asyāḥ grahaṇam kuru tvam vai puruṣa ratnam ca strī ratnam ca tu iyam satī yaḥ avirodha sukha tyāgī sa paśuḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kim tvam parīkṣase kāntam īdṛśam guṇinam sati devānām asurāṇām ca dānavānām vimardakam anena sārddham su ciram vihāram kuru sarvadā ante prāpsyati goloke śrī kṛṣṇam punar eva saḥ iti evam āśiṣam da tvā sva ālayam tu yayau vidhiḥ gāṃdharveṇa vivāhena jagṛhe tām ca dānavaḥ evam vivāhya tulasīm pituḥ sthānam jagāma ha iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍatapaḥkaraṇavivāhavarṇanam nāma aṣṭaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sva geham āgate tasmin śaṃkhacūḍe vivāhite tapaḥ kṛtvā varam prāpya mumuduḥ dānava ādayaḥ sva lokāt āśu nirgatya guruṇā svena saṃyutāḥ saḥ api dambha ātmajaḥ dṛṣṭvā gatam kula gurum ca tam praṇanāma mahā bhaktyā sa aṣṭāṃgam parama ādarāt atha śukraḥ kula ācārya om dṛṣṭvā āśiṣam anuttamam vṛttāṃtam kathayāmāsa deva dānavayoḥ tadā svābhāvikam ca tat vairam asurāṇām parābhavam vijayam nirjarāṇām ca jīva sāhāyyam eva ca dānava ādi asurāṇām tam adhipam vidadhe guruḥ tadā samutsavaḥ jātaḥ asurāṇām mudita ātma nām upāyanāni su prītyā daduḥ tasmai ca te akhilāḥ atha dambha ātmajaḥ vīraḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ pratāpavān rājya abhiṣekam āsādya sam reje surarāj tadā sa senām mahatīm karṣan daitya dānava rakṣasām ratham āsthāya tarasā jetum śakra purīm yayau vireje śaśi vaddhānām grahāṇām graha rāj iva āgacchantam śaṃkhacūḍam ākarṇya ākhaṇḍalaḥ svarāj tadā suraiḥ surāṇām ca saṃgrāmaḥ s tumulaḥ hi abhūt mahān kolāhalaḥ jātaḥ vīrāṇām garjatām raṇe parājayam ca saṃprāpuḥ asurāḥ dudruvuḥ bhayāt palāyamānān tān dṛṣṭvā śaṃkhacūḍaḥ svayam prabhuḥ yatra tatra sthitāḥ dīnāḥ girīṇām kaṃdarāsu ca tad adhīnāḥ na svataṃtrāḥ niḥprabhāḥ sāgarāḥ yathā saḥ api daṃbhāḥ tmajaḥ śūraḥ dānava indraḥ pratāpavān sura adhikārān saṃja sarva ālokān vijitya ca trailokyam sva vaśam cakre yajña bhāgān ca kṛtsnaśas babhūva api śāsitam nikhilam jagat kārayāmāsa vāyavyam adhikāram sva śaktitaḥ devāḥ nāma asurāṇām ca dānavānām ca rakṣasām gaṃdharvāṇām ca nāgānām kinnarāṇām rasaukasām trilokasya pareṣām ca sakalānām adhīśvaraḥ sa babhūva mahā vīraḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ mahā balī evam sa bubhuje rājyam rājarāja īśvaraḥ mahān sarveṣām bhuvanānām ca śaṃkha cūḍa śviram samāḥ tasya rājye na durbhikṣam na mārī na aśubha grahāḥ ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ nā eva sukhinyaḥ ca prajāḥ sadā a kṛṣṭa pacyā pṛthivī dadau sasyāni anekaśas oṣadhyaḥ vividhāḥ śvāsan sa phalāḥ sa rasāḥ sadā maṇi ākarāḥ ca nitarām ratna khanyaḥ ca sāgarāḥ sadā puṣpa phalāḥ vṛkṣāḥ nadyaḥ su salila āvahāḥ devān vinā akhilāḥ jīvāḥ sukhinaḥ nirvikārakāḥ sva svadharma āsthitāḥ sarve catur varṇa āśramāḥ pare bhrātṛ vaira tvam āśritya kevalam duḥkhinaḥ amarāḥ sa śaṃkhacūḍaḥ pravalaḥ kṛṣṇasya paramaḥ sakhā kṛṣṇa bhakti rataḥ sādhuḥ sadā go loka vāsinaḥ pūrva śāpa prabhāveṇa dānavīm yonim āśritaḥ tatas sura gaṇāḥ sarve hṛta rājyāḥ parājitāḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā vidhātāram natvā stutvā viśeṣataḥ brahmaṇe kathayāmāsuḥ sarvam vṛttāṃtam ākulāḥ brahmā tadā samāśvāsya surān sarvān munīn api taiḥ śva sārddham yayau loke vaikuṇṭham sukha dam satām dadarśa tatra lakṣmīśam brahmā deva gaṇaiḥ saha kirīṭinam kuṃḍalinam vanamālā vibhūṣitam aḥ sanaṃdana ādyaiḥ siddhaiḥ ca sevitam pīta vāsasam dṛṣṭvā viṣṇum surāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ sa muni īśvarāḥ praṇamya tuṣṭuvuḥ bhaktyā baddhāñjali karāḥ vibhum devāḥ ūcuḥ rakṣa asmān śaraṇa āpannān śrī hare trijagat varo tvam eva jagatām pātā triloka īśa acyuta prabho tat śrutvā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ brahmāṇam idam abravīt viṣṇuḥ uvāca kim kaṣṭam te samudbhūtam tat tvam vada mama agratas iti śrutvā hareḥ vākyam praṇamya ca muhur muhur baddhāñjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā vinaya ānata kandharaḥ vṛttāṃtam śaṃkhacūḍa kṛtam tadā deva kaṣṭa samākhyānam puras viṣṇoḥ parātmanaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca śaṃkhacūḍasya vṛttāṃtam sarvam jānāmi padmaja śṛṇu tad sarva vṛttāntam itihāsam purātanam saṃdehaḥ nā eva kartavyaḥ śam kariṣyati śaṅkaraḥ yatra saṃrājate śaṃbhuḥ para brahma para īśvaraḥ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya api yaḥ adhiṣṭhātā tri śakti dhṛk nirguṇaḥ sa guṇaḥ saḥ api param jyotiḥ yasya aṃga jāḥ tu vai brahmaḥ trayaḥ sṛṣṭi ādi kārakāḥ sattva ādi guṇa saṃpannāḥ viṣṇu brahma hāra abhidhāḥ tad samīpe ca golokaḥ gośālā śaṃkarasya vai tasya icchayā ca mad rūpaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vasati tatra ha tat bhavām rakṣaṇa arthāya tena ājñaptaḥ sadā sukhī tasya nārī samākhyātā rādhā iti prakṛteḥ paramā mūrtiḥ paṃcamī su vihāriṇī bahu gopāḥ ca gopyaḥ ca tatra saṃti tad aṃgajāḥ su vihāra parāḥ nityam rādhā kṛṣṇa anuvartinaḥ saḥ eva līlayā śaṃbhoḥ idānīm mohitaḥ anayā saṃprāptaḥ dānavīm yonim sudhā śāpāt sva duḥkha dām rudra śūlena tad mṛtyuḥ kṛṣṇena vihitaḥ purā śaṃkaram śaraṇam yāvaḥ sa sadyas śam vidhāsyati aham tvam ca amarāḥ sarvam tiṣṭhati iha visādhvasāḥ iti uktvā savidhiḥ viṣṇuḥ śiva lokam jagāma ha saṃsmara n manasā śaṃbhum sarva īśam bhakta vatsalam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍa vadha upākhyāne śaṃkhacūḍa rājya karaṇa varṇana pūrvaka tad pūrvabhavavṛttacaritravarṇanam nāma ekonatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śiva lokam mahā divyam nirādhāram abhautikam sāhādaḥ abhyantaram viṣṇuḥ jagāma su dita ānanaḥ saṃprāpya prathamam dvāram vicitram gaṇa sevitam dadarśa dvārapālān ca ratnā siṃhāsana sthitān śobhitā śveta vastraiḥ ca ratna bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitān triśūla ādi dharān vīrān bhasma rudra akṣa śobhitān sa brāhmaṇa rama īśaḥ ca tān praṇamya vinamrakaḥ kathayāmāsa vṛttāntam prabhu saṃdarśana arthakam tad ājñām ca daduḥ tasmai praviveśa tad ājñayā prabhu upakaṃṭha gati artham vṛttātam saṃnyavedayat tad dārapāya ca ājñaptaḥ tena anyam praviveśa ha evam paṃcadaśa dvārān praviśya kamalaḥ dbhavaḥ ājñaptaḥ ca śanais viṣṇuḥ viveśa abhyaṃtaram mudā sā pārṣadaiḥ parivṛtām lasat dehaiḥ su bhūṣitām maheśvarasya rūpaiḥ ca diś bhujaiḥ śubha kāntibhiḥ sat ratna yukta rudra akṣa bhasma ābharaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ nava indu maṃḍala ākārām catur asrām manoharām maṇi indra hāra nirmāṇa hīra sāra su śobhitām amūlya ratna racitām padma patraiḥ ca śobhitām māṇikya jāla mālābhiḥ nānā citra vicitritām padmarāga indra ra citām adbhutām śaṃkara icchayā indranīla maṇiḥ tam bhairva ṣṭitām su manoharām su saṃskṛtām ca sarvatra vāsitām gaṃdha vāyunā sahasra yojana āyāmām su pūrṇām bahu kiṃkaraiḥ dadarśa śaṃkaram sa aṃbam tatra viṣṇuḥ ssureśvaraḥ vasaṃtam madhyadeśe ca yathā indu tārakā vṛtam kirīṭinam kuṃḍalinam ratna mālā vi bhūṣitam puratas gīta nṛtyam ca paśyaṃtam sa smitam mudā devyā pradatta tāmbūlam bhuktavaṃtam su vāsitam gaṇaiḥ ca parayā bhaktyā sevitam śveta cāmaraiḥ stūyamānam ca siddhaiḥ ca bhakti namra ātma kaṃdharaiḥ guṇa atītam para īśānam trideva janakam vibhum nirvikalpam nirākāram sa ākāram sva icchayā śivam amāyam ajam ādyam ca māyā adhīśam parātparam prakṛteḥ puruṣasya api paramam sva prabhum sadā evam viśiṣṭam tam dṛṣṭvā paripūrṇatamam samam viṣṇuḥ brahmā tuṣṭuvatuḥ praṇamya sukṛta aṃjalī viṣṇu vidhī ūcatuḥ vayam te śaraṇa āpannāḥ rakṣa asmān duḥkhitāḥ vibho śaṃkhacūḍa ardita anviṣṭān sat nāthān parameśvara adhiṣṭhātā tasya vibhuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ayam tvad adhiṣṭhitaḥ pārṣada pravaraḥ tasya sudāmā deva yaṃtritaḥ rādhā śaptaḥ vabhūva atha śaṃkhacūḍaḥ ca dānavaḥ tena nissāritāḥ śaṃbho pīḍyamānāḥ samaṃtataḥ hṛta adhikārāḥ tridaśāḥ vicarānti mahī tale tvām vinā na sa vadhyaḥ ca sarveṣām tridivaukasām tam ghātaya maheśāna lokānām sa guṇaḥ ca sanniveśaḥ prakṛteḥ puruṣāt paraḥ rajasā sṛṣṭi samaye tvam brahmā sṛṣṭi kṛt prabho nitraiguṇye śiva ākhyātaḥ tuyyoṃ jyotiḥ svarūpakaḥ tvam dīkṣayā ca go loke tvam gavām paripālakaḥ tu a go śālā madhya gaḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ krīḍati aharniśam tvam sarva kāraṇam svāmī vidhiḥ viṣṇu īśvaraḥ param dīna anātha sahāyī ca dīnānām pratipālakaḥ dīna baṃdhuḥ triloka īśaḥ śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ virematuḥ śivam natvā karau baddhāḥ vinītakau iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe devadevastutiḥ nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ athā ākarṇya vacaḥ śaṃbhu īri vidhyoḥ su dīnayoḥ uvāca vihasan vāṇyā megha nāda gabhīrayā śivaḥ uvāca śaṃkhacūḍa udbhavam bhadram saṃbhaviṣyati asaṃśayam śaṃkhacūḍasya vṛttāṃtam sarvam jānāmi tattvataḥ kṛṣṇa bhaktasya gopasya sudānaḥ ca purā prabho mad ājñayā hṛṣīkeśo kṛṣṇa rūpam vidhāya ca go śālāyām sthitaḥ ramye go loke mad adhiṣṭhite svataṃtra ham iti svam sa moham matvā gataḥ purā tam dṛṣṭvā mohayati ugram tasya aham māyayā svayā teṣām saṃhatya sadbuddhi śāpam dāpitavān kila ittham kṛtvā sva līlām tām māyām saṃhṛtavān aham jñāna yuktāḥ tadā te tu mukta mohāḥ su buddhayaḥ samīpam āgatāḥ te me dīnībhūya praṇamya mām vṛttāṃta mavadan sarve lajjā ākulita mānasāḥ ūcuḥ mad puratas dīnāḥ rakṣa rakṣa iti vai giraḥ tadā tu aham bhavaḥ teṣām saṃtuṣṭaḥ proktavān vacaḥ bhayam tyajata he kṛṣṇa yūyam sarve mad ājñayā rakṣakaḥ aham sadā prītyā su bhadram vaḥ bhaviṣyati mad icchayā akhilam jātam idam sarvam na saṃśayaḥ sva sthānam gaccha tvam sārddham rādhayā pārṣadena ca dānavaḥ tu bhavet saḥ yam bhārate atra na saṃśayaḥ śāpa uddhāram kariṣye aham yuvayoḥ samaye khalu mad uktam iti saṃghārya śirasā rādhayā saha śrī kṛṣṇaḥ amodat atyantam sva sthānam agamat sudhīḥ nyaṣṭa ārtā sa bhayam tatra mad ārādhana tatparau sa sudāmā abhavat rādhā śāpataḥ dānava īśvaraḥ śaṃkhacūḍa abhidhaḥ deva drohī dharma vicakṣaṇaḥ kliśnāti su balāt kṛtsnam sadā deva gaṇam kudhīḥ mad māyā mohitaḥ saḥ uti duṣṭa maṃtri sahāyavān tat bhayam tyajata āśu eva mayi vai sati tasmin eva antare kṛṣṇaḥ rādhayā pārṣadaiḥ saha saṃmataḥ vidhinā prītyā saṃtasthau śiva śāsanāt tatas śaṃbhum punar natvā tuṣṭāva vihita añjaliḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ moha nirmuktaḥ jñātvā tattvam śivasya hi śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca kṣamasva ca aparādham me prasīda parameśvara sarve tvam nikhilāḥ dhīśa prasīda parameśvara tvam jyotiḥ paramam sākṣāt sarva vyāpī sanātanaḥ tvayā nāthena gaurīśa sa nāthāḥ sakalāḥ vayam tad phalam prāptavān asmi śāpam prāptaḥ sa vāmakaḥ pārṣada pravaraḥ yaḥ me sudāmā nāma gopakaḥ sa rādhā śāpataḥ svāmin dānavīm yonim āśritaḥ śāpa uddhāram kuruṣva adya pāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān iti uktvā rāma eva śrī kṛṣṇaḥ rādhayā saha śrī śivaḥ uvāca he kṛṣṇa gopikā nātha bhayam tyaja sukhī bhava mayā anugṛhṇatā tāta sarvam ācaritam tu idam sthātavyam sva adhikāre ca sāvadhāna tayā sadā viharasva yathākāmam mām vijñāya parātparam sva kāryam kuru rādheya pārṣadaiḥ khalu śāpa prabhāvam bhuktā vai punar āyāsyati svakam sudāmā pārṣadaḥ yaḥ hi tava kṛṣṇa priya priyaḥ dānavīm yonim āśritya idānīm kliśnāti vai jagat śāpa prabhāvāt vā adhāyāḥ devaśatruḥ ca dānavaḥ śaṃkhacūḍa abhidhaḥ saḥ ati daitya pakṣī suraguhaḥ tena nissāritāḥ devāḥ sa indrāḥ nityam prapīḍitāḥ hṛtāḥ dhikārāḥ vikṛtāḥ sarvam yātāḥ diśaḥ daśa brahma acyutau tad arthe hī śaraṇam mama teṣām keśa vinirmokṣam kariṣye na atra saṃśayaḥ iti uktvā śaṃkaraḥ kṛṣṇam punar provāca sādaram harim vidhim samābhāṣya vacanam kleśa nāśanam śivaḥ uvāca he hare he vidhe prītyā mama idam vacanam śṛṇu kailāsa vāsinam rudram mad rūpam pūrṇam uttamam deva kārya artham mud bhūtam pṛthak ākṛti dhāriṇam etad arthe hi mad rūpaḥ paripūrṇatamaḥ prabhuḥ saha iti śeṣaḥ cara acarāṇām sarveṣām sura ādīnām ca sarvadā iha api prāpnuyāt kaṣṭam putra pautra vivarjitaḥ rādhayā sahitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sva sthānam sa gaṇaḥ yayau muhur muhur praṇamya īśam vaikuṃṭha yayatuḥ hṛtam tān ādāya brahma viṣṇu kailāsam yayatuḥ girim tatra dṛṣṭvā maheśānam pārvatī vallabham prabhum dīna rakṣā ātta deham ca sa guṇam deva nāyakam tuṣṭuvuḥ pūrvavat sarve bhaktyā gadgadayā girā devāḥ ūcuḥ vayam tvām śaraṇa āpannā rakṣa devān bhaya ākulān śaṃkhacūḍa dānava indram jahi deva niṣūdanam tena vikāvitāḥ devāḥ saṃgrāme ca parājitāḥ hṛta adhikārāḥ ku tale vicaranti yathā narāḥ deva lokaḥ hi durhaśyaḥ teṣām āsīt ca tad bhayāt dīna uddhara kṛpā sindho devān uddhara saṃkaṭāt śakram bhayāt mahā īśāna hatvā tam dānava adhipam iti śrutvā vacaḥ śaṃbhuḥ devānām bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca vihasan vāṇyā megha nāda gabhīrayā śrī śaṃkaraḥ uvāca śaṃkhacūḍam vadhiṣyāmi sa gaṇam na atra saṃśayaḥ iti ākarṇya maheśasya vacaḥ pīyūṣa saṃnibham te sarve pramudā hi āsan naṣṭam matvā ca dānavam praṇipatya maheśam ca sura ādyāḥ sva padam yayuḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe śivopadeśaḥ nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha īśānaḥ mahā rudraḥ duṣṭa kālaḥ satām gatiḥ śaṃkhacūḍa vadham citte niścikāya sura icchayā dūtam kṛtvā citra ratham gaṃdharva aiśva śīghram prasthāpayāmāsa śaṃkhacūḍa aṃtike mudām sarva īśvara ājñayā dūtaḥ yayau tat nagaram ca saḥ gatvā dadarśa tad madhye śaṃkhacūḍa ālayam varam rājitam dvādaśa aiiri dvārapāla samanvitam sa dṛṣṭvā puṣpadantaḥ tu varam dvāram dadarśa saḥ kathayāmāsa vṛttāṃta dvārapālāya nirbhayaḥ atikramya ca tad dāram jagāma abhyaṃtare mudā atīva sundaram ramyam samalaṃkṛtam sa gatvā śaṃkhacūḍa tam dadarśa danuja adhipam dānava indraḥ parivṛtam sevitam ca tri koṭibhiḥ śata koṭi bhiḥ anyaiḥ śva bhramadbhiḥ śastra pāṇibhiḥ evaṃbhūtam ca tam dṛṣṭvā puṣpadaṃtaḥ sa vismayaḥ uvāca raṇa vṛttāṃta yat uktam śaṃkareṇa ca puṣpadaṃtaḥ uvāca rāja indra śiva dūtaḥ aham puṣpadaṃta abhidhaḥ prabho yat uktam śaṃkareṇa eva tat śṛṇu tvam bravīmi te śivaḥ uvāca rā jyam dehi ca devānām adhikāram hi sāṃpratam no ced kuru raṇam sārddham pareṇa ca mayā satām devāḥ mām śaraṇa āpannāḥ deveśam śaṃkaram satām aham kruddhaḥ mahā rudraḥ tvām vadhiṣyāmi asaṃśayam khala daṃḍa dharaḥ aham vai śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ rājyam dāsyasi kim vā tvam kariṣyasi raṇam ca kim puṣpadaṃtaḥ uvāca vitatham śaṃbhra vākyam na kadāpi danuja adhipa gatvā vakṣyāmi kim śaṃbho tathā tvam vada mām iha ittham ca puṣpadaṃtasya śiva dūtasya sat pateḥ ākarṇya vacanam rājā hasitvā tam u vāca saḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ uvāca rājyam dāsye na devebhyaḥ vīra bhogyā vasuṃdharā raṇam dāsyāmi te rudra devānām pakṣapātine atas pūrvam aham rudra tvām gamiṣyāmi asaṃśayam prabhāte āgamiṣyāmi vīra yātrā vicārataḥ tvam gaccha ā cakṣva rudrāya hi īdṛśam vacanam mama iti śrutvā śaṃkhacūḍa vacanam su prahasya saḥ rāja indra gaṇānām śaṃkarasya ca na sthātum saṃmukhe yogyaḥ kim punar tasya saṃmukham sa tvam dehi ca devānām adhikārāṇi sarvaśas śaṃkaraḥ paramātmā hi sarveṣām īśvara īśvaraḥ indra ādyāḥ ssakalāḥ devāḥ yasya ājñā vartinaḥ sadā sa prajāpatayaḥ siddhāḥ munayaḥ ca api ahi īśvarāḥ yasya bhrū bhaṃga mātreṇa sarveṣām pralayaḥ bhavet śivasya pūrṇa rūpaḥ ca loka saṃhāra kārakaḥ satām gatiḥ duṣṭa haṃtā nirvikāraḥ parātparaḥ avamānyāḥ na vai tasya śāsanam dānava ṛṣabha kim bahu uktena rāja indra manasā saṃvicārya ca rudram viddhi mahā eṃ śānam param brahma cit ātmakam dehi rājyam hi devānām adhikārān ca sarvaśas evam te kuśalam tāta bhaviṣyati anyathā bhayam iti śrutvā dānava indraḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ pratāpavān uvāca śiva dūtam tam bhavitavya vimohitaḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ uvāca svatas rājyam na dāsyāmi na adhikārān viniśvayāt kāla adhīnam jagat sarvam vijñeyam sacarācaram iti uktvā śiva dūtaḥ asau jagāma svāminam nijam yathārtha kathayāmāsa puṣpadaṃtaḥ ca sat mune iti śrī śivamahā tasya dūtasya tat vā kyam ākarṇya surarāj tatas sa krodhaḥ prāha giriśaḥ vīrabhadra ādikān gaṇān he vīrabhadra he naṃdin kṣetrapāla aṣṭa bhairavāḥ gaṇa aśva sannaddhāḥ sa āyudhāḥ bala śālinaḥ kumārābhyām saha eva adya nirgacchantu mama ājñayā śaṃkhacūḍa va dhārthāya nirgacchāmi adya sa tvaram iti ājñāpya maheśānaḥ niryayau sainya saṃyutaḥ sarve vīra gaṇāḥ tasya anuyayuḥ saṃpraharṣitāḥ vīrabhadraḥ ca nandī ca mahākālaḥ subhadrakaḥ viśālākṣaḥ ca bāṇaḥ ca piṃgalākṣaḥ vikaṃpanaḥ virūpaḥ vikṛtiḥ ca eva maṇibhadraḥ ca bāṣkalaḥ kapila ākhyaḥ dīrghadaṃṣṭraḥ vikaraḥ tāmralocanaḥ ityādayaḥ gaṇa īśānāḥ sainyānām patayaḥ varāḥ teṣām ca gaṇanām vacmi sāvadhāna tayā śṛṇu śaṃkha karṇaḥ koṭi gaṇaiḥ yutaḥ para vimardakaḥ daśabhiḥ vikṛtaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ eva ca catuṣṣaṣṭyā viśākhaḥ ca navabhiḥ pariyātrikaḥ ṣabhiḥ sarva antakaḥ śrīmān tathā eva vikṛta ānanaḥ jālakaḥ hi dvādaśābhiḥ koṭibhiḥ geṇa puṃgavaḥ saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubhaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ eva ca paṃcabhiḥ ca karālākṣaḥ ṣabhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ varaḥ koṭi koṭibhiḥ evā iha kaṃdukaḥ kuṃḍakaḥ tathā viṣṭaṃbhaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ eva iha gaṇapaḥ sarva sattamaḥ pippalaḥ ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ āveśanaḥ tathā aṣṭābhiḥ tu aṣṭābhiḥ candra tāpanaḥ mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaḥ vṛtaḥ kuṃḍī dvādaśabhiḥ vīraḥ tathā śubhaḥ kālaḥ ca kālakaḥ ca eva mahā kālaḥ śatena vai agnikaḥ śata koṭyā ca koṭyā agnimukhaḥ eva ca ādityaḥ hi arddha koṭyā ca tathā ca evam ghana āvahaḥ sanāhaḥ ca śate nā eva kumudaḥ koṭibhiḥ tathā amoghaḥ kokilaḥ ca eva śata koṭyā sumaṃtrakaḥ kākapādaḥ koṭi ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ tathā nīlaḥ navatyā deveśaḥ pūrṇabhadraḥ tathā eva ca koṭīnām ca eva saptānām caturvakaḥ mahā balaḥ koṭi koṭi saha trāṇām śataiḥ viṃśatibhiḥ tathā vīrabhadraḥ catuṣṣaṣṭyā lomajānām tri koṭibhiḥ kāṣṭhārūḍhaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sukeśaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tathā virūpākṣaḥ ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ tālaketuḥ ṣaṣ āsyaḥ ca paṃca āsyaḥ ca pratāpavān saṃvartakaḥ tathā caitraḥ laṃkulīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ loka aṃtakaḥ ca dīpta ātmā tathā daityāṃtakaḥ prabhuḥ devaḥ bhṛṃgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadeva priyaḥ tathā aśaniḥ bhānukaḥ ca eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasraśas kaṃkālaḥ kālakaḥ kālaḥ nandī sarvāntakaḥ tathā ete ca anye ca gaṇapāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mahā balāḥ yuddha artham niryayuḥ prītyā śaṃkhacūḍena nirbhayāḥ sarve sahasra hastāḥ ca jaṭāḥ mukuṭa dhāriṇaḥ candra rekhā avataṃsāḥ ca nīla kaṃṭhāḥ tri locanāḥ rudra akṣa ābharaṇāḥ sarve tathā asat bhasma dhāriṇaḥ hāra kuṃḍala keyūra mukuṭa acaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ brahma indra viṣṇu saṃkāśāḥ aṇima ādi guṇaiḥ vṛtāḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśāḥ pravīṇāḥ yuddha karmaṇi pṛthivī cāriṇaḥ kecid kecid pātāla cāriṇaḥ aṣṭau ca bhairavāḥ raudrāḥ ye vasavaḥ aṣṭau vāsava śva ādityāḥ dvādaśa te drutam hutāśanaḥ ca viśvakarmā aśvinau ca tau vāyuḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca eva budhaḥ ca maṃgalaḥ ca vai grahāḥ ca anye mahaśena kāmadevaḥ ca vīryavān ugradaṃṣṭra vāyadaṇḍaḥ koraṭaḥ koṭabhaḥ tathā svayam śata bhujā devī bhadrakālī maheśvarī ratnendra sāra nirmāṇa vimāna upari saṃsthitā rakta vastra parīdhānāḥ rakta mālya anulepanā nṛtyaṃtī ca hasaṃtī ca gāyaṃtī su svaram mudā bibhratī vikaṭām jihvām su lolām yojana āyatām śaṃkha cakra gadā padma khaṅga carma dhanuḥ śarān kharparam vartula ākāram gaṃbhīram yojana āyatam triśūlam gagana sparśa śaktim ca yojana āyatām vaiṣṇava astram vāruṇa astram vāyavyam nāgapāśakam nārāyaṇa astram gāṃdharva brahmāstram gāruḍam tathā pārjanyam ca pāśupatam jṛṃbhaṇa astram caṃ pārvatam mahāvīram ca sauram ca kālakālam mahānalam maheśvara astram yāmyam ca daṃḍam saṃmohanam tathā āgatya tasthau sā tatra yoginīnām tri koṭibhiḥ sārddham ca ḍākinīnām vai vikaṭānām tri koṭibhiḥ bhūta preta piśācāḥ ca kūṣmāṇḍāḥ brahmarākṣasāḥ vetālāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva yakṣāḥ ca eva sa kinnarāḥ taiḥ ca eva abhivṛtaḥ skaṃdaḥ praṇamya candraśekharam pituḥ pārśve sahāyaḥ yaḥ samuvāsa tad ājñayā atha śaṃbhuḥ samānīya sva sainyam sakalam tadā candrabhāgā nadī tīre vaṭa mūle manohare iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍa vadhe mahādevayuddhayātrāvarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ arthaḥ dhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca vidhitāta mahābuddhe mune jīva ciram samāḥ śiva dūte gate tatra śaṅkhacūḍaḥ ca dānavaḥ atha dūte gate tatra śaṅkhacūḍaḥ pratāpavān uvāca tulasīm vārtām gatvā abhyantaram eva tām śaṅkhacūḍaḥ uvāca śambhu dūta mukhāt devi yuddhāya aham samudyataḥ iti evam uktvā sa jñānī nānā bodhanataḥ priyām krīḍām cakāra harṣeṇa tām an ādṛtya śaṅkaram nānā kāma kalābhiḥ ca niśi cāṭu śataiḥ api brāhme muhūrte utthāya prātar kṛtyam vidhāya ca putram kṛtvā ca rāja indram sarveṣu dāneṣu ca priyām āśvāsayāmāsa sa rājā rudatīm punar niṣedhantīm ca gamanam nānā vārtā prakathya ca nija senāpatim vīram samāhūya samāhataḥ śaṅkhacūḍaḥ uvāca adya senāpate vīrāḥ sarve samara śālinaḥ daityāḥ ca dānavāḥ śūrāḥ ṣaḍaśītiḥ udāyudhāḥ kaṅkānām balinām śīghram senā niryātu nirbhayāḥ pañcāśat asurāṇām hi nirgacchantu kulāni vai koṭi vīryāṇi yuddha artham śambhunā deva pakṣiṇā sannaddhāni ca ghoṣrāṇām kulāni ca śatam drutam nirgacchantu raṇa artham hi śambhunā mama śāsanāt kālakeyāḥ ca mauryāḥ ca dauhṛdāḥ kālakāḥ tathā sajjāḥ niryāntu yuddhāya rudreṇa mama śāsanāt iti ājñāpya surapatiḥ dānava indraḥ mahā balaḥ tasya senāpatiḥ ca eva yuddha śāstra viśāradaḥ mahā rathaḥ mahā vīraḥ rathinām pravaraḥ raṇe tri lakṣa akṣauhiṇī yuktaḥ māṇḍalyam ca cakāra ha bahis babhūva śibirāt raṇe vīra bhayaṃkaraḥ ratna indra sāra nirmāṇam vimānam abhiruhya saḥ puṣpa bhadrā nadī tīre yatra akṣayavaṭaḥ śubhaḥ siddhāśrame ca siddhānām siddhikṣetram su siddhi dam kapilasya tapaḥ sthānam puṇya kṣetram ca bhārate śrīśaila uttara bhāge ca gandhamādana dakṣiṇe pañca yojana vistīrṇam dairghye śataguṇaḥ tathā śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśā bhārate ca su puṇya dā puṣpabhadrā nadī ramyā jala pūrṇā sarasvatī sarasvatī saṃśritā ca nirgatā sā himālayāt gomantam vāmatas kṛtvā praviṣṭā paścima udadhau tatra gatvā śaṅkhacūḍaḥ śivasenām dadarśa ha iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṇḍe śaṅkha cūḍayātrāvarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ dūtam kṛtvā mahā vijñam preṣayā māsa śaṃkaram sa tatra gatvām dūtaḥ ca candra bhālam dadarśa ha vaṭa mūle samāsīnam sūrya koṭi sama prabham kṛtvā yoga āsanam dṛṣṭayā mudrā yuktam ca sa smitam śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam brahma tejasā triśūla paṭṭiśa dharam vyāghra carma abara āvṛtam bhakta mṛtyu haram śatim gaurī kāntam trilocanam tapasām phala dātāram karttāram sarva saṃpadām āśu toṣam prasanna āsyam bhakta anugraha kātaram ca viśva bharam viśva karam viśva saṃhāra kāraṇam kāraṇam kāraṇānām ca naraka arṇava tāraṇam avaruhya rathāt dūtaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā dānava īśvaraḥ śaṃkaram sa kumāram ca śirasā praṇanāma saḥ loka āśiṣam dadau tasmai kālī skaṃdaḥ ca śaṃkaraḥ athā asau śaṃkhacūḍasya dūtaḥ parama śāstra vid uvāca śaṃkaram natvā karau baddhā śubham vacaḥ dūtaḥ uvāca śaṃkhacūḍasya dūtaḥ aham tvad sakāśam iha āgataḥ iti śrutvā ca vacanam śaṃkhacūḍasya śaṃkaraḥ prasanna ātmā mahādevaḥ bhagavān tam u vāca ha mahādevaḥ uvāca śṛṇu dūta mahā prājña vacaḥ mama sukha āvaham kathanīyām idam tasmai nirvivādam vicārya ca catvāraḥ te danoḥ putrāḥ dānavāḥ tejasā ulvaṇāḥ tasya tvam tanayaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ dharma ātmā dānava īśvaraḥ purā tvam pārṣadaḥ gopaḥ gopeṣu eva ca dhārmikaḥ adhunā rādhikā śāpāt jātaḥ tvam dānava īśvaraḥ dānavīm yonim āyātaḥ tattvataḥ na hi dānavaḥ nija vṛttam purā jñātvā deva varam tyaja adhunā na adhikam sa vikāram ca kuru rājyam vicārya ca dehi rājyam ca devānām mad prītim rakṣa dānava nija rājye sukham tiṣṭha tiṣṭhatu sva pade surāḥ kulīnāḥ śuddha karmāṇaḥ sarve kaśyapa vaṃśa jāḥ yāni kāni ca pāpāni brahmahatyā ādikāni ca jñāti droha ja pāpasya kalām na arhati ṣoḍaśīm ityādi bahuvāttau ca śruti smṛti parām śubhām śikṣita śaṃkhacūḍena sa dūtaḥ tarka vittamaḥ dūtaḥ uvāca tathyam kiṃcid yathārtha ca śrūyatām meṃ nivedanam tat kim īśa asurāṇām ca na surāṇām vada prabho śiraḥ chedam cakāra asau kasmāt cakrī maheśvara bhavān cakāra giriśaḥ surapakṣī iti viśrutam gṛhītvā tasya sarva svam kutas prasthāpitaḥ baliḥ sa bhrātṛkaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ katham devaiśva hiṃsitaḥ śuṃbha ādayaḥ asurāḥ ca eva katham devaiḥ nipātitāḥ purā samudra mathane pīyūṣam bhakṣitam suraiḥ krīḍā bhāṃḍam idam viśvam kālasya paramātmanaḥ deva dānavayoḥ vairam śaśvat naimittikam sadā parājayaḥ jayaḥ teṣām kāla adhīnaḥ krameṇa ca sura asurāṇām sarveṣām īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ iyam te rahitā lajjā sparddhā asmai bhissaha adhunā tava etat viparītam ca manasā saṃvicāryatām maheśaḥ uvāca vayam bhakta para adhīnāḥ na svataṃtrāḥ kadāpi hi tad icchayā tad karmāṇaḥ na kasya api ca pakṣiṇaḥ deva prārthanayā tena hiraṇyakaśipoḥ purā prahlāda artha vadhaḥ akāri bhaktānām hita kāriṇā deva prārthanayā akāri mayā api ca purā śrutam sarva īśvaryāḥ sarva mātu deva prārthanayā purā āsīt śubha ādibhiḥ yuddham vadhaḥ teṣām tayā kṛtaḥ adya api tridaśāḥ sarvam brahmāṇam śaraṇam yayuḥ hari brahma ādikānām ca prārthanā vaśatā upi aham surāṇām amī śvaraḥ dūta yuddha artham agamam khalu pārṣada pravaraḥ tvam hi kṛṣṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ ye ye hatāḥ ca daiteyāḥ na hi ke pi tvayā samāḥ devakayā arthim īśaḥ aham vinayena ca preṣitaḥ gaccha tvam śaṃkhacūḍe vai kathanīyam ca me vacaḥ iti uktvā śaṃkaraḥ tatra virarāma maheśvaraḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpu rāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe śivadūtasaṃvādaḥ nāma paṃcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ gatvā ca śiva vākyam jagāda ha tat śrutvā śaṃkhacūḍā asau dānava indraḥ pratāpavān aṃgīcakāra su prītyā raṇam eva sa dānavaḥ samāruroha yānam ca saha amātyaiḥ ca sa tvaraḥ ādideśa sva sainyam ca yuddha artha śaṃkareṇa ca śivaḥ sva sainyam devāṃśva prerayāmāsa sa tvaraḥ yuddha āraṃbhaḥ babhūva āśu neduḥ vādyāni bhūriśas saṃjātaḥ vīra śabdaḥ tathā eva ca svayam mahā indraḥ yuyudhe sārddham ca vṛṣaparvaṇā daṃbhena saha viṣṇuḥ ca cakāra paramam raṇam kāla asureṇa kālaḥ ca gokarṇena hutāśanaḥ bhayaṃkareṇa mṛtyuḥ ca saṃhāreṇa yamaḥ tathā kālambikena varuṇaḥ caṃcalena samīraṇaḥ budhaśva ghaṭa pṛṣṭhena raktākṣeṇa śanaiśvaraḥ jayantaḥ ratna sāreṇa vasavaḥ varcasām gaṇaiḥ aśvinau ca dhūmreṇa nalakūbaraḥ dhuraṃdhareṇa gaṇa kāṃkṣeṇa maṃgalaḥ śobhākareṇa vaiśvānaḥ pipiṭena ca manmathaḥ gokāmukhena cūrṇena khaḍga nānā sureṇa ca dhūmreṇa saṃhalena api viśvena ca pratāpinā palāśena dvādaśā arkāḥ yuyudhuḥ dharmataḥ pare asuraiḥ amarāḥ sārddham śiva sāhāyya śālinaḥ ekādaśa mahārudrāḥ ca ekādaśa bhayam karaiḥ mahāmaṇiḥ ca yuyudhe ca ugracaṃḍa ādibhiḥ saha rāhuṇā saha candraśva jīvaḥ śukreṇa dharmataḥ vaṭa mūle tadā śaṃbhuḥ tasthau kālyāḥ sutena ca ratna siṃhāsane ramye koṭi dānava saṃyutaḥ uvāsa śaṃkhacūḍaḥ ca ratna bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitaḥ nānā āyudhāni divyāni calati sma mahā mṛdhe gadaṣṭi paṭṭiśāḥ cakra bhuśuṃḍi prāsa mudgarāḥ nitriṃśa bhalla parighāḥ śaktayaḥ unmukha paraśvadhāḥ śara tomara khaṅgāḥ ca śatadbhyaḥ ca sahasraśas bhidipāla ādayaḥ ca anye vīra hasteṣu śobhitāḥ śirāṃsi cicchiduḥ ca ebhiḥ varāḥ tatra mahā utsavāḥ vīrāṇām ubhayoḥ ca eva sainyayoḥ garjatoḥ raṇe gajāḥ turaṃgāḥ bahavaḥ syandanāḥ ca padātayaḥ sa āroha vāhāḥ vividhāḥ taṃtra āsan su vikhaṃḍitāḥ nikṛtta bāhu ūru kara kaṭi karṇa yuga aṃtrayaḥ saṃchinna dhvaja bāṇa asi tanutra vara bhūṣaṇāḥ samu ddhata kirīṭaiḥ ca śirobhiḥ saha kuṃḍalaiḥ saṃraṃbha naṣṭeḥ āstīrṇā babhau bhūḥ karabha ūrubhiḥ sahasā paṭalaiḥ vā sa sāraṃghaiḥ mṛdhe bhaṭāḥ pradhāvantaḥ kabaṃdhān sva śira ukṣibhiḥ tarām vīrāḥ yuyudhuḥ ca parasparam vyanadan vīra saṃnnāda sa toyāḥ iva toyadāḥ sarvatas śara kūṭena vīraḥ sa ratha sārathim vīram saṃchādayāmāsa prāvṛṣ sūryam iva aṃbudaḥ āhvayantaḥ viśaṃtaḥ aye kṣipataḥ marmabhiḥ mithas sarvatas vīra saṃghāḥ ca nānā bāhu dhvaja āyudhāḥ vyadṛśyaṃta mahā saṃkhye kurvataḥ siṃha saṃravam sva śakhān ca vidadhmuḥ vai pṛthak pṛthak balganam cakrire taṃtra mahā vīrāḥ praharṣitāḥ babhūva yuddham vikaṭam karālam vīraṃharṣa dam līlā iyam śaṃkarasya parātmanaḥ yayā saṃmohitam sarvam sa deva asura mānuṣam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe parasparayuddhavarṇanam nāma paṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tadā deva gaṇāḥ sarve dānava aiśva parājitāḥ dudruvuḥ bhaya bhītāḥ ca śastra astra kṣata vigrahāḥ te parāvṛtya viśveśam śaṃkaram śaraṇam yayuḥ trāhi trāhi iti sarva īśa iti ūcuḥ vihvalayā girā dṛṣṭvā parājayam teṣām deva ādīnām sa śaṃkaraḥ sa bhayam vacanam śrutvā kopam uccais cakāra ha nirakṣyi sa kṛpā dṛṣṭayā devebhyaḥ śvā abhayam dadau balam ca sva gaṇānām vai varddhayāmāsa tejasā śiva ājñaptaḥ tadā skandaḥ dānavānām gaṇaiḥ saha kṛtvā krodham vīra śabdam devaḥ yaḥ tārakāṃtakaḥ akṣauhiṇīnām śatakam samare sa jaghāna ha rudhiram pātayāmāsa kālī kamala locanā teṣām śirāṃsi saṃchidya babhakṣa sahasā ca sā papau raktāni teṣām ca dānavānām samaṃtataḥ yuddham cakāra vividham sura dānava bhīṣaṇam śata lakṣam gaja indrāṇām śata lakṣam nṛṇām tathā kabaṃdhānām sahasram ca san nanarta raṇe bahu mahān kolāhalaḥ jātaḥ kkībānām ca bhayaṃkaraḥ punar skaṃdaḥ prakupya uccais śara varṣī cakāra ha pātayāmāsa kṣayataḥ koṭiśas asura nāyakān dānavāḥ śara jālena skandasya kṣata vigrahāḥ bhītāḥ praduvuḥ sarve śeṣāḥ mara ṇataḥ tadā vṛṣaparvā vipracitti daiśvā api vikaṃpanaḥ mahā mārī ca yuyudhe na babhūva parāṅmukhī babhūvuḥ te kṣata aṃga aśva skaṃda śakti prapīḍitāḥ mahāmārī skaṃdayoḥ ca vijayaḥ bhūt tadā sune neduḥ dudubhayaḥ svarge puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha skandaḥ sya samaram dṛṣṭvā mahā raudram tam adbhutam dānavānām kṣaya karam yathā prakṛti kalpakam mahā mārīkṛtam tat ca upadravam kṣaya hetukam cukopa atīva sahasā saṃnaddhaḥ bhūt svayam tadā varam vimānam āruhya nānā śastra astra saṃyutam abhayam sarva vīrāṇām nānā ratna paricchadam mahāvīraiḥ śaṃkhacūḍaḥ jagāma dhanuḥ vikṛṣya karṇa antam cakāra śara varṣaṇam tasya sā śara vṛṣṭiḥ ca durnivāryyā bhayaṃkarī mahā ghora aṃdhakāraḥ ca vadha sthāne babhūva ha devāḥ pradudruvuḥ sarve ye anye nandīśvara ādayaḥ parvatānām ca sarpāṇām nāgānām śākhinām tathā rājā cakāra vṛṣṭim ca durnivāryā bhayaṃkarīm tad dṛṣṭayā prahataḥ skandaḥ babhūva śiva nandanaḥ nīhāreṇa ca sāṃdreṇa saṃvṛtau bhāskarau yathā nānāvidhā sva māyām ca cakāra maya darśitām tām na avidan surāḥ kepi gaṇāḥ ca muni sattama tadā eva śaṃkhacūḍaḥ ca mahā māyī mahā balaḥ mayūram jarja rībhūtam divya astreṇa cakāra saḥ śakti cikṣepa sūrya ābhām tasya vakṣāse ghātinīm mūrcchām avāpa sahasā tad prahāreṇa sa kṣaṇa m punar ca cetanām prāpya kārtikaḥ para vīra hā smṛtvā pādau maheśasya sa ambi kasya ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ śastra astrāṇi gṛhītvā eva cakāra raṇam ulbaṇam sappaḥ ca parvatān ca eva vṛkṣān ca prastarān tathā sarvāḥ ciccheda kopena divya astre ṇa śiva ātmajaḥ vahnim nivārayāmāsa pārjanyena śareṇa ha ratham dhanuḥ ca ciccheda śaṃkhacūḍasya līlayā sannāham sarva vāhān ca kirīṭam mukuṭa ājvalam vīra śabdam cakāra asau jagarja ca punar punar cikṣepa śakti sūrya ābhām dānava indrasya vakṣāse muhūrta mātram tad kleśam vinīya sa mahā balaḥ śaktyā jaghāna tam ca api kārti keyam mahā balam sa papāta mahī pṛṣṭhe moghām kurvan vidhi pradām kālī gṛhītvā tam kroḍe nināya śiva sannidhau jñānena tam śivaḥ ca api jīva yāmāsa līlayā śaṃkhacūḍena yuyudhe samare bala śālinā vavarṣa samare astrāṇi yāni yāni ca dānavaḥ ciccheda līlayā vīraḥ tānitāni nija śaraiḥ divyāni astrāṇi śataśas mumuce dānava īśvaraḥ tāni ciccheda taṃbāṇaiḥ vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān athā atīva cukopa uccais śakha cūḍaḥ pratāpavān śaktyā jaghāna urasi tam sa cakaṃpe patāta kau kṣaṇena cetanām prāpya samuttasthau gaṇeśvaraḥ jagrāha ca dhanuḥ bhūyas vīrabhadraḥ gaṇāgraṇīḥ etasmin antare kālī jagāma samaram punar bhakṣitum dānavān rakṣitum kārtika icchayā vīrāḥ tām anujagmuḥ ca te ca nandīśvara ādayaḥ sarve deva aśva gaṃdharvāḥ yakṣāḥ rakṣāṃsi pannagāḥ vādya bhāṃḍāḥ ca bahuśas śataśas madhu vāhakāḥ punar samudyatāḥ ca āsan vīrā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe śaṃkhacūḍavadhe sa sainya śaṃkhacūḍayuddhavarṇanam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sā ca gatvā hi saṃgrāmam siṃhanādam cakāra ha devyāḥ ca tena nādena mūcchīm āpuḥ ca dānavāḥ aṭṭaṭṭahāsam aśivam cakāra ca punar punar tadā papau ca mādhvīkam nanarta raṇa mūrddhani ugradaṃṣṭrā ca ugradaṃḍā koṭavī ca papau madhu anyāḥ ca devyaḥ tatra ājau nanṛtuḥ madhu saṃpaṣuḥ mahān kolāhalaḥ jātaḥ gaṇadeva dale tadā dṛṣṭvā kālīm śaṃkhacūḍaḥ śīghram ājau samāyayau dānavāḥ ca bhayam prāptāḥ rājā tebhyaḥ abhayam dadau rājā jaghāna tam śīghram vaiṣṇava aṃkita līlayā nārāyaṇa astram sām devī cikṣepa tad upari aram vṛddhim jagāma tat chatram dṛṣṭvā vāmam ca dānavam tam dṛṣṭvā śaṃkhacūḍaḥ ca pralaya agni śikhā upamam papāta daṃḍa vat bhūmau praṇanāma punar punar nivṛttim prāpa tat chatram dṛṣṭvā namram ca dānavam tam dṛṣṭvā prajjvalaṃtam ca praṇamya bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ brahmāstreṇa dānava indraḥ vinirvāram cakāra haṃ atha kruddhaḥ dānava indraḥ dhanuḥ ākṛṣya raṃhasā jagarja sa aṭṭahāsam ca dānavāḥ bhayam āyayuḥ kālyai cikṣepa śaktim sa śata yojanam āyatām devī divya astra jālena śata khaṃḍam cakāra sā sa ca vaiṣṇavam astram ca cikṣepa caṃḍikā upari māheśvareṇa kālī ca vinivāram cakāra sā prekṣakāḥ abhavana sarve devāḥ ca dānavāḥ api atha kruddhā mahā devī kālī kāla samā raṇe jagrāha mantra pūtam ca śaram pāśupatam ruṣā kṣepāt pūrvam tat niṣeddhum vāc babhūva aśarīriṇī na kṣipa astram imam devi śaṃkhacūḍāya vai ruṣā mṛtyuḥ pāśupatāt moghāt api ca caṃḍike śaṃkhacūḍasya vīrasya upāyam anyam vicāraya śata lakṣam dānavānām jaghāsa līlayā kṣudhā attum jagāma vegena śaṃkhacūḍam bhayaṃkarī divya astreṇa ca raudreṇa vārayāmāsa dānavaḥ grīṣma sūrya upamam tīkṣṇa dhāram atyanta bhīkaram sā kālī tam samālokya āyatim prajjvalitam ruṣā prasārya mukham āhāram cakre tasya ca paśyataḥ divyāni astrāṇi ca anyāni ciccheda dānava īśvaraḥ prāptāni pūrvatas cakre śata khaṃḍāni tāni ca sarva siddha īśvaraḥ śrīmān aṃtardhānam cakāra saḥ vegena muṣṭinā kālī tam a dṛṣṭvā ca dānavam athā aṃgatya drutam māyī cakram cikṣepa vegataḥ bhadrakālyai śaṃkhacūḍaḥ pralaya agni śikhā upamam sā devī tam tadā cakram vāma hastena līlayā jagrāha sva mukhena eva āhāram cakre ruṣā drutam muṣṭayā javāna tam devī mahā kopena vegataḥ babhrāḥ ma dānava indraḥ upi kṣaṇam mad śam avāpa saḥ cetanām prāpya sacā uttasthau pratāpavān na cakre bāhu yuddham ca mātṛ buddhayā tayā saha gṛhītvā dānavam devī bhrāmayitvā punar punar ūrddha ca prāpayāmāsa mahā kopena vegataḥ utpapāta ca vegena śaṃkhacūḍaḥ pratāpa vān aruroha sa
