su pra ṇamya rahaḥ dūtaḥ śaṃkarasya kṛta aṃjaliḥ naṃdīśvaraḥ uvāca draṣṭum icchati devi tvām devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ sva vallabhām rūpa kṛtām mayā uktam deśataḥ tatas tad vacanāt vaurī maṃḍanam kartum ādarāt udyatā abhūt muni śreṣṭha pativrata parāyaṇā āgacchāmi prabhum gaccha vada tam tvam mama ājñayā ājagāma tatas naṃdī rudra āsannam manogatiḥ vāḍham uktvā sa tām gatvā gaurīm āha su locanām draṣṭum icchati te bhartā kṛta veṣām manoramām śaṅkaraḥ bahudhā devi vihartum saṃpratīkṣate evam labdha bhāvaḥ yathā sadyas pārvatyāḥ darśana utsukaḥ ayam pinākī kāmāriḥ vṛṇuyāt yām nitaṃbinīm sarvāsām divya nārīṇām rājñī bhavati vai dhruvam vīkṣaṇam gauri rūpeṇa krīḍayet manmathaiḥ gaṇaiḥ kāmaḥ ayam iṃtim kāmārim ūcuḥ anyonyam āhatāḥ spaṣṭam śaknoti yā dākṣāyaṇī striyam sāṃgacche tatra niśśaṃkam mohayet pārvatīpatim kūṣmāṃḍa tanayām tatra śaṃkaram spraṣṭum utsahe aham gaurī surūpeṇa citralekhā vacaḥ travīt yat adhāt mohinī rūpam keśavaḥ mohana icchayā purā tat vaiṣṇavam yogam āśritya paramārthataḥ urvaśyāḥ ca tatas dṛṣṭvā rūpasya parivartanam kālī rūpam ghṛtācī tu viśvācī cāṃḍikam vapuḥ raṃbhā ca gāyatram menakā tathā sa hajanyā jayā rūpam vaijayam puṃjaka sthalī mātṛṇām api anuktānām anuktāḥ ca apsarovarāḥ yatnāt rūpāṇi anu tatas tāsām tu rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā kuṃbhāṃḍa naṃdinī vaiṣṇavāt ātma yogāt ca vijñāta arthāḥ vyaḍaṃbayan ūṣā bāṇāsurasutā divya yoṃ ga viśāradā cakāra rūpam pārvatyāḥ divyam ati adbhutam śubham mahā rakta abja saṃkāśam caraṇam ca uktam aprabham divya lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam manaḥ abhīṣṭa artha dāyakam tasyāḥ ramaṇa saṃkalpam vijñāya girijā tatas uvāca sarva vijñānā sarva antaryāminī śivā svaārṣaḥ svarūpam iti śeṣaḥ yatas mama sva rūpam vai dhṛta mūṣe sakhi tvayā asmin tu kārtike māsi ṛtu dharmāḥ tu mādhave dvādaśyām śuka pakṣe tu yaḥ tu ghore niśāṃgame kṛta upavāsīm tvām bhoktā suptām aṃtar pure naraḥ ā bālyāt viṣṇu bhaktā asi yatas aniśa mataṃdvitā atha sā pārvatī devī kṛta kautuka maṃḍanā rudra saṃnidhim āgatya cikrīḍe tena śaṃbhunā tatas rata aṃte bhagavān udraśvā darśanam yayau iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām paṃcame yuddha khaṇḍe ūṣācaritravarṇanam śivaśivāvivāhavarṇanam nāma ekapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇuṣva anyat caritram ca śivasya paramātmanaḥ purā bāṇāsuraḥ nāma daiva doṣāt ca garvitaḥ kṛtvā tāṃḍava nṛtyam ca toṣayāmāsa śaṃkaram jñātvā saṃtuṣṭa manasam pārvatī vallabham śivam uvāca ca asuroḥ bāṇaḥ nata skandhaḥ kṛta aṃjaliḥ bāṇaḥ uvāca tvad prasādāt valī ca aham śṛṇu meṃ paramam vacaḥ bāhūnām giri tulyānām vinā yuddham vṛṣadhvajam purāṇi ācūrṇayan advīn bhītāḥ te api pradudruvuḥ mayā yamaḥ kṛtaḥ yoddhā vahniḥ vai kṛtakaḥ mahān varuṇaḥ ca api gopālaḥ gavām pālayitā tathā gajādhyakṣaḥ kuberaḥ tu sairandhrī ca api nirṛtiḥ jita śva ākhaṇḍalaḥ loke kara dāyī sadā kṛtaḥ śatru hasta prayuktaiḥ śva śastra astreḥ jarjarīkṛtāḥ patantu śatru hastāt vā pātayantu sahasradhā kṛtvā abravīt mahā manyuḥ bhakta bādhā apahārakaḥ darpasya asya praśamanam lapsyase ca āśu dāruṇam tatra te giri saṃkāśāḥ bāhavaḥ anala kāṣṭha vat chinnām bhūmau patiṣyati śastra astraiḥ kadalīkṛtāḥ yat eṣa mānuṣa śiraḥ mayūra sahitaḥ dhvajaḥ vidyate tava duṣṭa ātman tasya syāt patanam yadā sthāpitasya āyudhāgāre vinā vāta kṛtam bhayam tadā yuddham mahā ghoram saṃprāptam iti nidhāya ghoram saṃgrāmam gacchethāḥ sarva sainyavān tathā mahā utpātān tatra dṛṣṭvā asi durmate praṇamya ca mahādevam bāṇaḥ ca sva gṛham gataḥ kuṃbhaṇḍāya yathāvṛttam pṛṣṭaḥ provāca harṣitaḥ paryaikṣiṣṭa asuraḥ bāṇaḥ tam yogam hi utsukaḥ sadā dṛṣṭvā tatra asuraḥ bāṇaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ yuddhāya niryayau sa sva sainyam samāhūya saṃyuktaḥ sa aṣṭabhiḥ gaṇaiḥ iṣṭim sāṃgrāmikām kṛtvā dṛṣṭvā sāṃgrāmikam madhu iti hṛd kamale kṛtvā kaḥ kasmāt āgamiṣyati yoddhā raṇa priyaḥ yastuḥ nānā śastra astra pāragaḥ tathā śastraiḥ mahā tīkṣṇaiḥ china etasmin antare kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ śaṃkareṇa hi yatra sā bāṇa duhitā sujātā kṛta maṃgalā mādhavam mādhave māsi pūjayitvā mahāniśi suptā ca tiḥpure gupte strī bhāvam upalaṃbhitā gauryā saṃpreṣitena api vyākṛṣṭāḥ divya māyayā kṛṣṇa ātmaja ātmajena atha rudaṃtī sāhi anātha vat sa ca api tām balāt bhukkā pārvatyāḥ sa khibhiḥ punar nītaḥ tu divya yogena dvārakām nimiṣa aṃtarāt mṛditā sā tadā utthāya rudaṃtī vividhāḥ giraḥ sakhībhyaḥ kathayitvā tu dehatyāge kṛtakṣaṇā sakhyā akṛtātmanaḥ doṣam sā vyāsa smāritā punar sarvam tad pūrva vṛttāṃtam tatas dṛṣṭvā ca sā abhavat ūṣā bāṇasya tanayā kuṃbhāṃḍa tanayā mune uṣā uvāca sākha yadi eṣa me bhartā pārvatyām vihitaḥ purā iti ūṣā vacanam śrutvā sakhī provāca tām tadā tvayā svapne ca yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ devi tam katham aham samānayiṣyāmi na vijñātaḥ tu yaḥ mama daitya kanyā tat ukte tu rāga aṃdhā maraṇa utsukā rakṣitā ca tayā sakhyā prathame divaseṃ tatas punar provāca sā uṣām vai citralekhā mahāmatiḥ kuṃbhāṃḍasya sutāḥ bāṇa tanayām muni sattama vyasanam te apakarṣāmi trilokyām yadi bhāṣyate samāneṣya naram yaḥ te manohartā tam ādiśa iti uktvā vastra puṭake devān daityān ca dānavān gandharva siddha nāgān ca yakṣa ādīn ca tathā alikhat tathā naraḥ teiṣu vṛṣṇīn śūram ānakaduṃdubhim āsīdavā sakhi aśi śkīti vibhāvaḥ ārṣaḥ iḍā ārṣaḥ ūṣā provāca cauraḥ asau mayā prāptaḥ tu yaḥ niśi puruṣaḥ sakhi yena āśu cetaḥ ranam hṛtam mama yasya saṃsparśanāt evam mohitā aham tathā abhavam tam aham jñātum icchāmi vada sarvam ca bhāmini iti uktā sā abravīt nām yoginī tasya ca anvayam utsukā bāṇa tanyā babhāṣe sā tu kāminī ūṣā uvāca upāyam racaya prītyā tad prāptyai sakhim tad kṣaṇāt yena upāyena tam kāntam labheya prāṇa vallabham yam vinā aham kṣaṇam nā ekam sakhi jīvitum utsahe iti uktvā sā tayā bāṇa ātmajayā maṃtri kanyakā vismitā abhūt muni śreṣṭha su vicāra parā abhavat tatas sakhīm samābhāṣya citralekhā manojavā buddhā tam kṛṣṇa pautram sā dvārakām gaṃtum udyatā jyeṣṭha kṛṣṇa caturdaśyām tṛtīye tu gate ahani ā prabhātāt muhūrte tu saṃprāptāḥ dvārakām purīm ekena kṣaṇa mātreṇa nabhasām divya yaḥ ginī tatas ca aṃtaḥpura udyāne prādyumniḥ dadṛśe tayā krīḍan nārī janaiḥ sārddham prapiban mādhavī madhu sarva aṃga sundara śyāmaḥ su smitaḥ nava yauvanaḥ tatas khām samārūḍham aṃdhakāra paṭena sā tatas sā mūrdhni tām khayam gṛhītvā nimiṣa aṃtarāt saṃprāptā yatra sā bāṇanaṃdinī kāma ārtā vividhān bhāvān cakāra unmatta mānasā ānītam atha tam dṛṣṭvā tadā bhītā ca sā abhavat yāvat krīḍitum ārabdham tāvat jñātam ca tad kṣaṇāt iṃgitaiḥ anumā naiḥ ca kanyā dauḥśīlyam ācaran taruṇaḥ darśanīyaḥ tu sāhasī samara priyaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sarva mā ācakhyuḥ bāṇāya vali sūnave puruṣāḥ te mahā vīrāḥ kanyā antaḥpura rakṣakāḥ dvārapālāḥ ūcuḥ deva kaścid na jānīte guptaḥ catiḥpure balāt śakraḥ tu tava kanyām vai svayaṃgrāhāt adharṣayat teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā dānava indraḥ mahā balaḥ vismitaḥ abhūt muni śreṣṭha kanyāyāḥ śruta dūṣaṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahā purāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām paṃcame yuddha khaṇḍe ūṣācaritravarṇanam nāma dvipañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā vismitam vākyam kim kāraṇam atha abravīt bāṇaḥ krodha parītā hasan iva aho manuṣyaḥ rūpa āḍhayaḥ sāhasī dhairyavān iti duṣṭa bhāgyaḥ vimūḍha dhīḥ yena me kula cā ritram dūṣitam duhitā hitā tam mārayadhvam kupitāḥ śīghram śastraiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ durācāram ca tam baddhā ghore kārā gṛhe tatas rakṣadhvam vikaṭe vīrāḥ bahukāḥ laṃ viśeṣataḥ vadhāya tasya vīrasya vyādiṣṭam pāpa buddhinā tad ādiṣṭāḥ tu te vīrāḥ puram drutam chādayāmāsuḥ ati ugrāḥ chiāgha bhiṃdi iti vādinaḥ śatru sainyam tatas dṛṣṭvā garjamānaḥ sa yādavaḥ antaḥpuram dvāra gatam parigham gṛhya ca atulam niṣkrāṃtaḥ bhavanāt tasmāt vajra hastaḥ iva aṃtakaḥ tena tān kikarān hatvā punar catas puram yayau jaghāna roṣa rakta akṣaḥ varddhitaḥ śiva tejasā lakṣe hate atha yodhānām tatas bāṇa asuraḥ ruṣā kuṃbhāṃḍam sa gṛhītvā tu yuddhe śauṃḍam samāhvayat tatas daśa sahasrāṇi turaṃgāṇām ratha uttamān tad vadhāya tatas śaktim kāla vaiśvānara upamām aniruddhaḥ gṛhītvā tām tayā tam nijaghāna hi rathopasthe tatas bāṇaḥ tena śaktyā hataḥ dṛḍham sa sa aśvaḥ tad kṣaṇam vīraḥ tatra eva antaradhīyata adṛśyamānaḥ tu tadā kūṭa yodhaḥ sa dānavaḥ nānā śastra sahasraiḥ tam jaghāna hi punar punar chadmanā nāgapāśaiḥ tam babaṃdha sa mahā balaḥ bali putraḥ mahā vīraḥ śiva bhakta śśara asuraḥ tam badhvā paṃjara aṃtastham kṛtvā yuddhāt upāramat uvāca bāṇaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ sūtaputram mahā balam bāṇāsuraḥ uvāca yena me dūṣitam pūtam balāt duṣṭena sat phalam chitvā tu sarva gātrāṇi rākṣasebhyaḥ prayaccha bhoḥ atha asya rakta māṃsāni kravyādāḥ api bhuṃjatām agādhe tṛṇa saṃkīrṇe kūpe pātakinam jahi kim bahu uktyā sūtaputra māraṇīyaḥ hi kuṃbhāṃḍaḥ tu atravīt vākyam bāṇam san maṃtri sattamam kuṃbhāṃḍaḥ uvāca ayam tu dṛśyate deva tulyaḥ viṣṇoḥ parākramaiḥ imām avasthām prāptaḥ asi pauruṣe saṃvyavasthitaḥ ayam śiva prasādāt vai kṛṣṇa pautraḥ mahā balaḥ asmān tṛṇa upamān vetti daṣṭaḥ api bhujagaiḥ valāt etat vākyam tu vāṇāya kathayitvā sa dānavaḥ kuṃbhāṃḍaḥ uvāca kena vā tvam iha ānītaḥ durācāra nara adhama daitya indram stuhi vīram tvam namaskuru kṛtāṃjaliḥ jitaḥ asmi iti vacaḥ dīnam kathayitvā punar punar evam kṛte tu mokṣaḥ syāt anyathā baṃdhana ādi caṃ niśācara durācāra śatru dharme na vetsi bhoḥ dainyam palāyanam ca atha śūrasya maraṇa adhikam kṣatriyasya raṇe śreyaḥ maraṇam sat mukhe sadā na vīra māninaḥ bhūmau dīnasya iva kṛtāṃjaliḥ ityādi vīra vākyāni bahūni sa jagāda tam tat ākarṇya sa bāṇaḥ sām vismitaḥ abhūcukopa ca tadā uvāca nabhaḥ vāṇī bāṇasya āśvāsanāya hi śṛṇvatām sarva vīrāṇām aniruddhasya maṃtriṇaḥ vyomavāṇī uvāca śivaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ sākṣī karmaṇām parama īśvaraḥ saḥ eva kartā bhartā ca saṃhartā jagatām sadā sarvasya aṃtargataḥ svāmī prerakaḥ sarvatas paraḥ nirvikāri avyayaḥ nityaḥ māyā adhīśaḥ api nirguṇaḥ nāśayiṣyati te garvam idānīm bhakta vatsalaḥ iti ābhāṣya nabhaḥ vāṇī virarāma mahā mune bāṇā suraḥ tad vacanāt aniruddham na jaghnivān mad vākyam ca visasmāra vijahāra viruddha dhīḥ priyayā atṛpta cetāḥ tu durgām sasmāra tad kṣaṇāt āgaccha me kuru trāṇam yaśode caṃḍa roṣiṇī śiva bhakte mahādevi sṛṣṭi sthiti aṃta kāriṇī tvām vinā rakṣakaḥ nā anyaḥ stasmāt rakṣa śive hi mām tena ittham toṣitā tatra kālī bhinna aṃjana prabhā jyeṣṭha kṛṣṇa caturdaśyām saṃprāptā āsīt mahā niśi gurubhiḥ muṣṭi nighataiḥ dārayāmāsa paṃjaram śarān tān bhasmasātkṛtvā sarpa rūpān bhayānakān mocayitvā aniruddham tu tatas ca aṃtaḥpuram tatas praveśayitvā durgā tu tatra eva adarśanam gatā ittham devyāḥ prasādāt tu śiva śakteḥ muni īśvara prādyumniḥ vāṇa tanayām priṃyoṃ prāpya sumoda ca pūrvavat vijahām rāsaum tayā sva priyayā sukhī pīta pānaḥ su rakta akṣaḥ sa bāṇa sutayā tatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe ūṣācaritre aniruddhoṣāvihāravarṇanam nāma tripaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tayā kṛṣṇaḥ kim akārṣīt hi tat vada śrutvā ca vyathitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ babhūva muni sattama apaśyatām ca aniruddham tad badhūnām hareḥ tathā catvāraḥ vārṣikāḥ māsāḥ vyatīyuḥ anuśocatām nāradāt tat upākarṇya vārtā baddhasya karma ca āsanmu vyathitāḥ sarve vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇa devatāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tad vṛttam akhilam śrutvā yuddham na ca ādarāt jagāma śoṇitapuram tārkṣyamā hūya tad kṣaṇāt pradyumnaḥ yuyudhānaḥ ca sāraṇaḥ naṃda upanaṃda bhadra ādyāḥ rāmakṛṣṇa anuvartinaḥ akṣauhiṇībhiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ sametāḥ ssarvatas diśam rurudhuḥ bāṇa nagaram samaṃtāt sātvata ṛṣabhāḥ bhajyamāna pura udyāna prakāra aṭṭāla gopuram vīkṣyamāṇaḥ rūpa āviṣṭaḥ tulya sainyaḥ rabhiniryayau bāṇa arthe bhagavān rudraḥ sa sutaḥ prathamaiḥ vṛtaḥ āsīt su tumulam yuddham adbhutam śoma harṣaṇam kṛṣṇa ādikānām taiḥ tatra rudra ādyaiḥ bāṇa rakṣakaiḥ kṛṣṇa śaṃkarayoḥ āsīt pradyumna guyoḥ api kūṣmāṃḍa kūpa karṇābhyām balena saha sam yugaḥ sāṃbasya bāṇa putreṇa bāṇena saha sātyakeḥ nandinā garuḍasya api pareṣām ca paraiḥ api brahma ādayaḥ sura adhīśāḥ munayaḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ gaṃdharva apsarasaḥ yānaiḥ vimānaiḥ draṣṭum āgaman yuddham babhūva vipra indra teṣām ca yadu vaṃśi nām bhratrā rāmeṇa sahitaḥ pradyumnena ca dhīmatā samaram atulam pramathaiḥ saha pramathaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ teṣām atyaṃta dāruṇam yuddham babhūva vikaṭam vṛṣṇīnām roma harṣaṇam vibhīṣikābhiḥ vahvībhiḥ koṭarībhiḥ pade pade nirlajjābhiḥ ca nārībhiḥ prabalābhiḥ adūrataḥ śaṃkara anucarān śauriḥ bhūta pramatha guhyakān drāvayāmāsa tīkṣṇa āyaiḥ śaraiḥ śārṅga dhanuḥ cyutaiḥ cakruḥ yuddham mahā ghoram śatru sainyam vināśayan viśi ryamāṇam sva balam dṛṣṭvā rudra uti amarṣaṇaḥ tat śrutvā śaṃkara gaṇāḥ vineduḥ yuyudhuḥ ca te mardayan pratiyoddhāram varddhitāḥ śaṃbhu tejasā pṛthagvidhāni ca ayukta śāstrāṇi pinākine pratyakṣaiḥ śamayāmāsa śūlapāṇiḥ avismitaḥ āgneyasya ca pārjanyam naijam nārāyaṇasya ca kṛṣṇa sainyam vidudrāva prativīreṇa nirjitam vidrāvite sva sainye tu śrī kṛṣṇaḥ ca param tapaḥ svam jvaram śītala ākhyam hi vyasṛjat vāruṇam mune vidrāvite kṛṣṇa sainye kṛṣṇasya śītalajvaraḥ maheśvaraḥ atha tam dṛṣṭvā ayāntam svam visṛjat jvaram māheśvaraḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ ca yuyudhāte jvarau ubhaiau vaiṣṇavaḥ atha samākraṃdat māheśvara bala arditaḥ viṣṇu śītajvaram prāha śaraṇa āgata vatsalaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā caritam kṛṣṇaḥ visismāya bhaya anvitaḥ jaghāna śaktyā pradyumnam daitya saṃgha ati amarṣaṇaḥ asṛ gvimuṃcan gātrebhyaḥ balena apākramat raṇāt kuṃbha aṃḍa kūpa karṇābhyām nānā astraiḥ ca samāhataḥ kṛtvā sahasram kāyānām pītvā toyam mahā arṇavāt garuḍaḥ nāśayati atha megha arṇava aṃbuṣu vegena mahatā aram vai śṛṃgābhyām nijaghāna tam śṛṃga ghāta viśīrṇa āgaḥ garuḍaḥ atīva vismitaḥ vidudrāva vihāya ca janārdanam evam jāte caritram tu bhagavān devakī sutaḥ uvāca sārathim śīghram rudra teja uti vismitaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca he sūta śṛṇumat vākyam ratham me vāhaya drutama mahādeva samīpa sthaḥ yathā syām gaditum vacaḥ iti uktaḥ hariṇā sūtaḥ dārukaḥ sva guṇa agraṇīḥ drutam tam vāhayāmāsa ratham rudra samīpataḥ atha vijñāpayāmāsa nataḥ bhūtvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ śaṃkaram bhaktyā prapannaḥ bhakta vatsalam śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca namāmi tvā anantaśakti sarvātmānam para īśvaram viśva utpatti sthāna nāśa hetum brahma liṃgam param śatim kevalam parameśvaram kṣetram ca prāṇaḥ ātmā ca vikāraḥ tad samūhakaḥ līlayā eva svīkṛtaiḥ nirjara ādikān lokaśas nūnam vibharṣi haṃsi unmārgān svabhāvataḥ tvam hi brahma param jyotiḥ gūḍham brahmaṇi vāc maye yam mala ātmānam ākāśam iva kevalam tvam eva ca ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ advitīyaḥ taryaḥ ātma dṛś īśaḥ hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca sa vikāraḥ pratīyase yathā eva sūryo pihitaḥ chāyā rūpāṇi ca prabho su acchā yayā saṃcakāsti hi ayam parama dṛś bhavān guṇena apihitaḥ api tvam guṇena eva guṇān vibho sva pradīpaḥ cakāsti tvam bhūman giriśa śaṃkara tvad maya āmohita dhiyaḥ putra dāra gṛha ādiṣu yaḥ tvad pādau sa śocyaḥ hi ātma vaṃcakaḥ tvad ājñayā aham bhagavān bāṇa doḥ chettum āgataḥ tu athā eva śaptaḥ bāṇaḥ ayam garvitaḥ garva hāriṇā ājñām dehi prabho me tvam bāṇasya bhuja kṛṃtane iti ākarṇya vacaḥ śaṃbhuḥ śrī kṛṣṇasya muni īśvaraḥ pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā kṛṣṇa stutyā maheśvaraḥ satyam uktam tvayā tāta mayā śaptaḥ hi daitya rāj mad ājñayā bhavān prāptaḥ bāṇa dos daṃḍa kṛtane kim karomi ramānātha bhakta adhīnaḥ sadā hare paśyataḥ me katham vīra syāt vāṇa bhuja kṛṃtanam atas tvam jṛṃbhaṇa astreṇa mām jṛṃbhaya mad ājñayā tatas tvam kuru kārya svam yatheṣṭam ca sukhī bhava iti uktaḥ śaṃkareṇa atha śārṅgapāṇiḥ su vismitaḥ svaraṇa sthānam āgatya mumoda sa muni īśvaraḥ jṛṃbhaṇa astram mumoca atha saṃdhāya dhanuṣi drutam pinākapāṇaye vyāsa nānā astra kuśalaḥ hariḥ mohayitvā tu giriśam jṛṃbhaṇa astreṇa jṛṃbhitam bāṇasya pṛtanām śauriḥ jaghāna asi ga daṣṭibhiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām paṃcame yuddha khaṃḍe bāṇa amurarudrakṛṣṇādiyuddhavarṇanam nāma catuḥ paṃcāśattamaḥ a dhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca adbhutā iyam kathā tāta śrāvitā me tvayā sune jṛṃbhite jṛṃbhaṇa astreṇa hariṇā samare hare hate vāṇa bale bāṇaḥ kim akārṣīt ca tat vada sūtaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vyāsa mahā prājña kathām ca parama adbhutām kṛṣṇa śaṃkarayoḥ tāta loka līlā anusāriṇoḥ vāṇaḥ vinirgataḥ yuddham kartum kṛṣṇena daitya rāj kuṃbhāṃḍa saṃgṛhītāḥ vaḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā nija balam naṣṭam sa daitya indraḥ ati amarṣitaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ api mahā vīraḥ giriśa āpta mahā balaḥ uccais jagarja tatra ājī vāṇam mattvā tṛṇa upamam dhanuḥ ṭaṃkārayāmāsa śārgāṃkhyam nijam adbhutam trāṃsa kakud doṣaṇī iti bhāṣya udāharaṇāt dās śabdasya napuṃsaka tvam yat bāṇa sainyam tat avaśiṣṭam muni īśvara tena nādena mahatā dhanuḥ ṭaṃkāra jena hi dyāvābhūmyoḥ aṃtaram vai vyāptam āsīt anaṃtaram cikṣepa vivi dhān bāṇān bāṇāya kupitaḥ hariḥ karṇa antam tat vikṛṣya atha tīkṣṇān āśīviṣa upamān āyātaḥ tān nirīkṣya atha sam bāṇaḥ bali nandanaḥ tatra sum vṛṣṇayaḥ sarvam kṛṣṇa ātmānaḥ vicetasaḥ smṛtvā śiva pada ambhojam cikṣepa nija sāyakān sa kṛṣṇāya ati śūrāya mahāgava baleḥ sutaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ api tān asaṃprāptān acchinat sva śaraiḥ drutam smṛtvā śiva pada ambhojam amarāriḥ mahā balaḥ rāma ādayaḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ ca sva svam yoddhāram āhave babhūva tumulam yuddham śṛṇvatām vismaya āvaham bāṇa asura balam pakṣa āghātaiḥ amardayat marditam sva balam dṛṣṭvā mardayaṃtam ca tam balī cukopa ati baleḥ putraḥ śaiva rāj ditija īśvaraḥ cikṣepa yugapad vāṇān amitān tatra vīra hā garuḍe ca pṛthak pṛthak jaghāna ekena garuḍam kṛṣṇam ekeṇa patriṇā tatas kṛṣṇaḥ viṣṇu rūpaḥ surāri hā jaghāna bāṇam tarasā śārṅga nissṛta sat śaraiḥ ciccheda tat dhanuḥ śīghram chatra ādi kamanā ākulaḥ hayāḥ ca pātayāmāsa hatvā tān sva śaraiḥ hariḥ kṛṣṇam jaghāna gadayā saḥ apatat dharaṇī tale utthāya āram tatas kṛṣṇaḥ yuyudhe tena śatruṇā śiva bhaktena devarṣe loka līlā anusārataḥ evam dvayoḥ ciram kālam babhūva su mahān raṇaḥ śiva rūpaḥ hariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sa ca śaiva uttamaḥ balī kṛṣṇaḥ atha kṛtvā samaram ciram bāṇena vīryavān śiva ājñayā muni īśvaraḥ tatas sudarśanena āśu kṛṣṇaḥ bāṇa bhujān bahūn ciccheda bhagavān śaṃbhu śāsanāt para vīra hā avaśiṣṭāḥ bhujāḥ tasya catvāraḥ atīva sundarāḥ gata vyathaḥ babhūva āśu śaṃkarasya prasādataḥ gata smṛtiḥ yadā bāṇaḥ śira chet tam samudyataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vīra tvam āpannaḥ tadā rudraḥ samutthitaḥ bhagavan devakīputra yat ājñaptam mayā purā tat kṛtam ca tvayā vipra mad ājñā kāriṇā sadā māḥ bāṇasya śiraḥ chidhi saṃhara sva su darśanam dadhīce rāvaṇe vīre tārakā ādi pureṣu api vinā mad ājñām lakṣmīśa rathāṅgam na amucaḥ purā tvam tu yogi īśvaraḥ sākṣāt paramātmā janārdana vicāryatām sva manasā sarva bhūta hite rataḥ bhujān kaṇḍūyamānaḥ tu vismṛta ātma garti hare tadā aham aśapam tam vai bhuja chettā āgamiṣyati mad ājñayā hariḥ prāptaḥ bhuja chettā tava atha vai iti uktaḥ sa tayoḥ maitrīm kārayitvā maheśvaraḥ tad anujñāpyaḥ sa gaṇaḥ sva putram sva ālayam yayau iti ākarṇya vacaḥ śaṃbhoḥ saṃhṛtya ca sudarśanam akṣata aṃgaḥ tu vijayī tat kṛṣṇā uṃtaḥpuram yayau aniruddham samāśvāsya sahitam bhāryayā punar jagrāha ratna saṃghātam bāṇadattam anekaśas tad sakhīm citralekhām ca gṛhītvā para yoginīm prasannaḥ abhūt tatas kṛṣṇaḥ kṛta kāryaḥ śiva ājñayā hṛdā praṇamya giriśam āmaṃtrya ca baleḥ sutam dvārakām ca purīm prāptaḥ samutsavam amanvitaḥ visarjayitvā garuḍam sakhīn vīkṣya upahasya ca dvārakāyām tatas dṛṣṭvā kāma cārī cacāra ha iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām paṃcame yuddha khaṃḍe bāṇabhujakṛta nagarvāpahāravarṇanam nāma pañcapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇe gate dvārakāyām aniruddhena bhāryayā tatas bāṇaḥ tattvam vada mahā mune kṛṣṇe gate dvārakāyāḥ maniruddhena bhāryayā duḥkhitaḥ abhūt tatas bāṇaḥ sva ajñānam saṃsmaran hṛdā tatas nandī bāṇam provāca duḥkhitam daityam śoṇita digdha aṃga manu tāpa samanvitam nandīśvaraḥ uvāca bāṇa śaṃkara sat bhakta mā anutāpam kuruṣva bhoḥ bhakta anukaṃpī śaṃbhuvai bhakta vatsala nāmadhṛk manyasva bhakta śārdūla śivam smara punar punar bhakta anukaṃpanaḥ ca asya śaṃkarasya punar punar nandi vākyāt tatas bāṇaḥ dviṣā śīrṣaka mātrakaḥ śiva sthānam jagāma āśu dhṛtvā dhairye mahāmanāḥ gatvā tatra prabhum natvā ruroda atīta vihvalaḥ gata garva trajaḥ bāṇaḥ premā kulita mānasaḥ nana tāṃḍavam mukhyam pratyālīḍha ādi śobhitam mukha vāda sahasrāṇi bhrū kṣepa sahitāni api śiraḥ kampa sahasrāṇi prāpta anīkaḥ sahasraśas vārīḥ ca vividha ākārāḥ darśayitvā śanais śanais tathā śoṇita dhārābhiḥ siñcayitvā mahī talam rudra prasādayāmāsa śūlinam candraśekharam bāṇa asuraḥ mahā bhaktaḥ vismṛta ātma gatiḥ mamaḥ uvāca bāgam saṃhṛṣṭaḥ vāṇa tāta baleḥ putra saṃtuṣṭaḥ nartanena te bāṇena saṃvṛṇītaḥ abhūiṃraiḥ tu vraṇa ropaṇe uṣā putrasya rājyam tu tasmin śoṇitaka āhvaye nirvaira tā ca vibudhaiḥ viṣṇunā ca viśeṣataḥ na punar aidaitya tā duṣṭā rajasā tamasā yutā śaṃbhu bhaktiḥ viśeṣeṇa nirvikārā sadā mune śiva bhakteṣu ca snehaḥ dayā sarveṣu jaṃtuṣu iti kṛtvā varān śaṃbho bali putraḥ suraḥ premṇā anayanaḥ rudram tuṣṭāva su kṛta aṃjaliḥ bāṇaḥ uvāca tvām namāmi mahā īśāna dīna bandho dayā nidhe kṛtā mayi kṛpā atīva kṛpā sāgara śaṃkara brahmāṃḍa tanuḥ ugra īśaḥ virāj sarva anvitaḥ paraḥ te manaśū andraḥ tava prabho jaṭharam vārddharbhujā iṃdraḥ dhiṣaṇā vidhiḥ romāṇi auṣadhayaḥ nātha keśāḥ jala mucaḥ tava guṇāḥ trayaḥ tri netrāṇi sarva ātmā puruṣaḥ bhavān brāhmaṇam te mukham prāhuḥ bāhum kṣatriyam eva ca vaiśyam āhuḥ te pāda jam śūdram eva ca yaḥ tvām visṛjate martyaḥ ātmānam priyam īśvaram viṣṇuḥ brahmā vibudhāḥ munayaḥ vā amala āśayāḥ sarva ātmanā prapannāḥ tvām śaṃkaram priyam īśvaram tatas śaṃbhoḥ prasādena mahākāla tvam āgataḥ iti kila śara nāmnā śaṃkarasya api vṛttam sakala guru janānām sam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhi tāyām paṃ yuddhakhaṃḍe bāṇāsuragaṇapatvaprāptivarṇanam nāma ṣaṭpaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahā premṇā caritam śaśimau linaḥ yathā avadhī triśūlena dānava indram gaja asuram devānām ca hita arthāya purā sukham yayuḥ tasya putraḥ mahā vīraḥ muni īśvara gaja asuraḥ pituḥ vadham hi saṃsmṛtya kṛtam devyā sura arthanāt vidhi prītyā tatāpa paramam tapaḥ avadhyaḥ aham bhaviṣyāmi strīpuṃsaiḥ kāma nirjitaiḥ saṃvicārya eti manasā abhūt tapaḥ rata mānasaḥ sa tepe himavat roṇyām tapaḥ parama dāruṇam ūrddhabāhuḥ nabhaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ pāda aṃguṣṭha āśrita avaniḥ jaṭā bhāraiḥ sa vai reje pralaya arkaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ mahiṣa asura putraḥ a sau gaja asuraḥ udāra dhīḥ nipetuḥ sa grahāḥ tārāḥ jajjvaluḥ ca diśaḥ daśa tena taptāḥ surāḥ sarve divam tyaktvā sa vāsavāḥ brahma lokam yayuḥ vijñāpayāmā su śvacāla bhūḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ na śaknumaḥ divi sthātum atas te śaraṇam gatāḥ vidhehi upa śamam tasya ca anyān jīvayitum kṛpā lokāḥ naṃkṣyati anyathā hi satyam satyam bruvāmahe iti vijñāpitaḥ devaiḥ vāsava ādyaiḥ saḥ ātmabhūḥ tapaṃtam tapasā lokān yathā abhra apihitam divi vilakṣya vismitaḥ prāha vihasan sṛṣṭi kārakaḥ prāptaḥ aham vara daḥ tāta varam vṛṇu yathā īpsitam utthāya utthāya daitya indra īkṣamāṇaḥ dṛśā vibhum rā gadgadayā prītaḥ agṛṇāt devam sa māhiṣiḥ gajāsuraḥ uvāca avadhyaḥ aham bhaveyam vai strīpuṃsaiḥ kāma nirjitaiḥ sarveṣām lokapālānām nikhila ddhi subhuj vibho evam vṛtaḥ śa ta dhṛtiḥ dānavena sa tena vai evam labdha varaḥ daityaḥ māhiṣiḥ ca gaja asuraḥ sa vijitya diśaḥ savām lokān ca trīn mahā asuraḥ deva asura manuṣya indrān gaṃdharva garuḍa uragān ityādīn nikhilān jitvā vaśa mānī viśvajit jahāra lokapālānām sthānāni saha tejasā deva udyāna śriyā juṣṭam adhyāste sma triviṣṭapam mahā indra bhavanam sākṣāt nirmitam viśva karmaṇā reme abhivaṃdya aṃtri yugaḥ sura ādibhiḥ pratāpitaiḥ ūrjita caṃḍa śāsanaḥ saḥ ittham nirjita kakubh ekarāj viṣayān priyān yathopajoṣam bhuṃjānaḥ na atṛpyat ajita indriyaḥ kāle vyatīte pāpa buddhiḥ abhūt tatas mahiṣa asura putraḥ asau saṃcikkeśa dvijān varān tāpasān nitarām pṛthvyām dānavaḥ sura mardanaḥ surān narān ca pramathān sarvān cikkeśa durmatiḥ dharma anvitān viśeṣeṇa pūrva vairam anusmaran agaccha drājadhānī vai śaṃkarasya gajāmuraḥ trāta trāta iti tatra āsīt ānaṃda vana vāsinām mahiṣā asa tasmin avasare devāḥ śaka ādyāḥ tad parājitāḥ śivasya śaraṇam jagmuḥ natvā tuṣṭuvuḥ ādarāt nyavedayan dānavasya tasya kāśyām samāgamam keśa ādhikyam tatratyānām tad nāthānām viśeṣataḥ deṣā ūcuḥ kaṣṭam datte tvad janānām tam jahi tvam kṛpā nidhe yatra yatra dharāyām ca caraṇam pramiṇoti hi acalām sa calām tatra karoti nija bhārataḥ yasya dos daṃḍa ghātena cūrṇīsyuḥ ca śiloccayāḥ nīlimānam na ca adya api jaghuḥ stad keśa saṃga jam yasya viśvāsasam bhāraiḥ uttaraṃgāḥ mahā abdhayaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi nava yasya samucchrayaḥ yat netrayoḥ piṃgalimā tathā taralimā punar yām yām diśam samabhyeti saḥ ayam dussaha dānavaḥ avadhyaḥ aham bhavāmi itim strīpuṃsaiḥ kāma nirjitaiḥ rakṣasvam bhaktān deveśa kāśī rakṣaṇa tatparaḥ tatra ājagāma soram tad badha kāmanayā haraḥ āgatam tam samālokya śaṃkaṭa bhakta vatsalam triśūla hastam garjatam jagarja sa gaja asuraḥ tatas tayoḥ mahān āsīt samaraḥ dāruṇaḥ adbhutaḥ nānā astra śastra saṃpātaiḥ vīra ārāvam prakurvatoḥ vivyādha giriśam bāṇaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ dānava ghātinam tat śarān cicchide pūrṇam aprāptaḥ tilaśas mune tatas triśūla hetiḥ tam āyāntam daitya puṃgavam vijñāya avadhyam anyena śūlena abhijaghāna tam gajāsuraḥ uvāca jāne tvām tridiva īśāna triśūlin smara hāriṇam aṃdhakāre maheśāna tripurāṃtaka sarvaga kiṃcid vijñaptum icchāmi tat śṛṇuṣva kṛpā kara satyam bravīmi na a satyam mṛtyuṃjaya vicāraya vikatthate iti śeṣaḥ jagatām vaṃdyaḥ viśvasya upari saṃsthitaḥ kālena sarvaiḥ martavyam śreyase mṛtyuḥ īdṛśaḥ iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tasya śaṃkaraḥ karuṇā nidhiḥ prahasya pratyuvāca īśaḥ māhiṣeyam gaja asuram īśvaraḥ uvāca gaja asura prasannaḥ asmi sva anukūlam varam vṛṇu pratyuvāca prasanna ātmā vā indraḥ gaja asuraḥ gajāsuraḥ uvāca imām kṛttim maheśāna tva triśūla anipāvitām sukha sparśā raṇa aṃgaṇa paṇīkṛtām darśanīyām mahā divyām sarvadā eva sukha āvahām iṣṭa gaṃdhiḥ sadā eva astu sadā eva astu ati komalā sadā eva nirmalā ca astu sadā eva astu ati maṃḍanām mahā tapaḥ nala jvālām prāpya api su ciram vibho na dagdhā kṛttiḥ eṣā me puṇya gaṃdha nidheḥ tatas yadi puṇyavatī nā eṣā mama kṛtti diś aṃbara tadā tvad aṃga saṃgaḥ usyāḥ katham jātaḥ raṇa aṃgaṇe anyam ca me varam dehi yadi tuṣṭaḥ asim śaṃkara nāma astu kṛttivāsāḥ te prārabhya adyatanam dinam tathā iti uvācam su prītaḥ maṃhiṣa asura jam ca tam punar provāca prīta ātmā dānavam tam gaja asuram īśvaraḥ uvāca idam puṇyam śarīram te kṣetre asmin mukti sādhane kṛttivāseśvaram nāma mahāpātaka nāśanam sarveṣām eva liṃgānām śiraḥ bhūtam vimukti dam gaja asurasya mahatīm prāvṛṇot hi diś aṃbaraḥ harṣam āpuḥ janāḥ sarve kāśī sthāḥ pramathāḥ tathā hari brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ harṣa nirbhara mānasāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ tam maheśānam natvā sajila yaḥ tatas yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt prītyā śrāvayet vā śuci vrataḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe gajāsuravadhaḥ nāma saptapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa pravakṣyāmi caritam śaśimaulinaḥ yathā duṃdubhi nirhrādam avadhīt itijam haraḥ viṣṇu devena kālena prāpa duḥkham mahat ditiḥ sāṃtvayāmāsa tām vāgbhiḥ duḥkhitām nā ārṣaḥ kha daḥ atha daityaḥ sa māyāvī ditim āśvāsya daitya rāj devāḥ katham su jeyāḥ syuḥ iti upāyam aciṃtayat devaiḥ ca ghātitaḥ vīraḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ viṣṇunā ca saha bhrātrām sa chalaiḥ daitya vairibhiḥ kiṃbalāḥ ca kimāhārāḥ kimādhārāḥ hi nirjarāḥ mayā katham su jñeyāḥ tyuḥ iti upāya maciṃtayat brāhmaṇān haṃtum asakṛt anvadhāvata vai tatas yatas kratu bhujaḥ devāḥ kratavaḥ veda saṃbhavāḥ te vedāḥ brāhmāṇā ādhārāḥ tatas deva balam dvijāḥ niścitam brāhmaṇa ādhārāḥ sarve vedāḥ sa vāsavāḥ gīrvāṇāḥ brāhmaṇa balāḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā brāhmaṇāḥ yadi naṣṭāḥ syuḥ vedāḥ naṣṭāḥ te svayam atas teṣu praṇaṣṭeṣu vinaṣṭāḥ satatam surāḥ yajñeṣu nāśam gacchatsu hata āhārāḥ tatas surāḥ āhariṣyāmi devānām akṣayāḥ sarva saṃpadaḥ nirvekṣyāmi sukhāni eva rājye nihata kaṃṭake dvijāḥ kva saṃti bhūyāṃsaḥ brahma tejaḥ ūti bṛṃhitāḥ bhūyasām brāhmaṇānām tu sthānam vārāṇasī khalu tām ādau upasaṃhṛtya yāyām tīrtha ataram tatas iti duṃdubhi nirhrādaḥ mārtam kṛtvā kula ucitām prāpya api kāśīm durvṛttaḥ māyāvī nyavadhīt dijānan samidh kuśān samādātum yatra yānti dvijottamāḥ vane vanecaraḥ bhūtvā yādaḥ rūpaḥ jalāśaye adṛśya rūpī māyāvī devānām api agocaraḥ yāminyām vyāghra rūpeṇa ā bhakṣayat brāhmaṇān bahūn niśśaṃkam bhakṣayati evam na tyajati api kīkaśam ittham nipātitān tena viprāḥ duṣṭena bhūriśas vyāghra rūpam samāsthāya tam ādātum matim dadhe tam bhaktam dhyānam āpannam dṛḍha cittam śiva īkṣaṇe kṛta astra mantra vinyāsam tam krāṃtum aśakat na saḥ atha sarva gataḥ śambhu jña tvā tasya āśayam haraḥ yāvat āditsati vyāghraḥ tāvat āvirabhūt haraḥ jagat rakṣāḥ bhaveyuḥ iti śeṣaḥ bhakta rakṣaṇa dakṣa dhīḥ rudra māyā aṃtam ālokyaḥ tad bhakta ācita liṅgataḥ sa avajñam atha sarva jñam yāvat paśyati dānavaḥ tāvat āyātam ādāya kakṣāyaṃtre nyapīḍayat paṃcāsyaḥ tu atha paṃcāsyam muṣṭayā mūrddhani atāḍayat sa tena muṣṭi ghātane kakṣa niṣpeṣaṇena ca ati ārta māra dvaya āmraḥ rodasī pūrayan mṛtaḥ tena nādena mahatā saṃpravepita mānasāḥ tapodhanāḥ samājagmuḥ niśa śabda anusārataḥ atra īśvaram samālokya kakṣīkṛta mageśvaram tuṣṭavuḥ praṇatāḥ ssarve śarve jaya jaya akṣaraiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ūcuḥ paritrātāḥ paritrātāḥ pratyūhāt dāruṇāt itas anugraham kuruṣva īśa tiṣṭha atra eva jagadguro ane nā eva sva rūpeṇa vyāghreśaḥ iti nāmataḥ kuru rakṣām mahādeva jyeṣṭhasthānasya sarvadā duṣṭān gaurīśa bhaktebhyaḥ dehi ca abhayam iti ākarṇya vacaḥ teṣām bhaktānām candraśekharaḥ yaḥ mām anena rūpeṇa drakṣyati śraddhayā atra vai tasya upasarga saṃdhānam pātayiṣyāmi asaṃśayam mad caritram idam śrutvā smṛtvā liṃgam idam hṛdi saṃgrāme praviśan mati om jayam āpnoti asaṃśayam etasmin aṃtare devāḥ samājagmuḥ sa vāsavāḥ praṇamya śaṃkaram premṇā sarve sāṃjalayaḥ surāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ etad dudubhi nirhrāda vadhā trātāḥ vayam surāḥ sadā rakṣā prakartavyā bhaktānām bhakta vatsala vadhyāḥ khala aśva deveśa tvayā sarva īśvara prabho iti ākarṇya vacaḥ teṣām surāṇām parameśvaraḥ te api viprāḥ mahā harṣāt punar yātāḥ yathāgatam śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet vā api paṭhet vā pāṭhayet tathā idam ākhyānam atulam śiva līlā amṛta akṣaram param bhakti pradam dhanyam śiva prīti karam śivam parama jñāna dam ramyam vikāra haraṇam param iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvi rudrasaṃhitāyām pañca yuddha khaṇḍe duṃdubhinirhrādadaityavadhavarṇanam nāma aṣṭapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa su saṃprītyā caritam parimeśituḥ yathā avadhīt sva priyayā daityam uddiśya sam jñayā āstām purā mahā daityau vidala utpala saṃjñakau tṛṇīkṛta trijagatī puruṣābhyām lāt tābhyām sarve surāḥ brahman daityābhyām nirjitāḥ raṇe tābhyām parājitāḥ devāḥ vidheḥ te śaraṇam gatāḥ natvā tam vidhivat sarvam kathayāmāsuḥ āda rāt dhairyam kuruta saṃsmṛtya sa śivam śivam ādarāt bhakta vatsala nāmā asau sa śivaḥ śam karaḥ śivaḥ śam dīrgheṇa kālena parameśvaraḥ iti uktvā tān tatas brahmā tūṣṇīm āsīt śivam smaran te api devāḥ mudam prāpya sva svam dhāma yayuḥ tadā atha nārada devarṣiḥ śiva preraṇayā tadā gatvā tadīya bhavanam śivā sauṃdaryam ājagau śrutvā tad vacanam daityāḥ vā āstām māyā vimohitau devīm parijihīṣū tau viṣama iṣu prapīḍitau vicārayāmāsatuḥ tau kadā kutra śivā ca sā bhaviṣyati vidheḥ prāpta udayā nnau iti sarvadā kautukena eva cikrīḍe śivā kaṃduka līlayā udaṃcatī aṃcat aṅgānām lāghavam paritanvatī niśśvāsa āmoda mudita bhramara ākulita īkṣaṇā sphuṭat cola aṃśuka patha tiryad aṃga prabhā vṛtā ullasat kaṃduka āsphāla ati śroṇita kara ambujā bhrū latā aṃcalā mṛḍānī kilaḥ khelaṃtī dadṛśe jagadambikā aṃtarikṣa carābhyām ca ditijābhyām kaṭā kṣitā kroḍīkṛtābhyām iva vai samupasthita mṛtyunā vidala utpala saṃjñābhyām dṛptābhyām varataḥ vidheḥ tṛṇīkṛta trijagatī puruṣābhyām sva dos balāt devīm tām saṃjihīrṣatā viṣama iṣu prapīḍitau divaḥ utteratuḥ kṣipram māyām svīkṛtya śāṃbarīm dhṛtvā māyā māyātau aṃbikā antikam tau atyaṃtam su durvṛttau ati caṃcala mānasau atha duṣṭa nihaṃtrā vai sa avajñena hareṇa tau vijñātau ca kṣaṇāt āstām kaṭākṣitā atha devena dugā durgati ghātinī daityau imau iti gaṇau na iti sarva svarūpiṇā atha sā netra saṃjñām sva svāḥ minaḥ tām bubodha ha mahā kautukinaḥ tāta śaṃkarasya para īśituḥ tatas vijñāya saṃjñām tām sarvajña arddha śarīriṇī mahā balau mahādevyā kaṃṭukena samāhatau daṃbholinā parihate śṛṃge iva mahā gireḥ tatas pariṇatim yātaḥ liṃga rūpeṇa kaṃdukaḥ kaṃdukeśvara saṃjñām ca tat liṃgam abhavat tadā jyeṣṭheśvara samīpe tu sarva duṣṭa nivāraṇam śiva āvirbhāvam ājñāya vṛṣayaḥ ca samāyayuḥ atha sarve surāḥ śambhoḥ varān prāpya tad ājñayā sva dhāmāni yayuḥ prītāḥ tathā kāśī nivāsinaḥ sa aṃbikam śaṃkaram dṛṣṭvā kṛtām jali puṭāḥ ca te praṇamya tuṣṭuvuḥ bhaktyā vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ ādarāt sa vikaḥ api śivaḥ vyāsa krīḍitvā su vihāra vid jagāma sva ālayam prītaḥ sa gaṇaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ kaṃdukeśvara liṃgam ca kāśyām duṣṭa nivarhaṇam idam ākhyānam atulam śṛṇuyāt yaḥ mudā anvitaḥ śrāvayet vā paṭhet yaḥ ca tasya duḥkha bhayam kutas śivayoḥ bhakta vātsalya sūcakam śiva dam satām iti uktvā āmaṃtrya tam vyāsam tad nutaḥ mad vara ātmajaḥ yayau vihāyasā kāśīm caritam śaśimaulinaḥ iyam hi saṃhitā raudrī sampūrṇā varṇitā mayā imām yaḥ ca paṭhet nityam śatru bādhā nivārikām sarvān kāmān avāpnoti tatas muktim labheta nā sūtaḥ uvāca iti brahma suta śrutvā pitrā śiva yaśaḥ param śata nāmā āpya śaṃbhoḥ ca kṛtārthaḥ abhūt śiva anugaḥ brahma nārada samvādaḥ sampūrṇaḥ kathitaḥ mayā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcame yuddha khaṃḍe vidalotpaladaityavadhavarṇanam nāma ekonaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ yam yuddha khaṃḍaḥ samāptā iyam dvitīyām rudra saṃhitā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dvitīyāyām rudrasaṃhitāyām pañcamaḥ yuddha khaṇḍaḥ samāptaḥ samāptā iyam dvitīyā rudra saṃhitā
